## 现在时

1 am/is/are 

2 am/is/are (疑问句)

3 I am doing (现在进行时)

4 are you doing? (现在进行时的疑问式)

5 I do/work/like 等 (一般现在时)

6 I don't ... (一般现在时的否定式)

7 Do you ...? (一般现在时的疑问式)

8 I am doing (现在进行时) 与 I do (一般现在时) 比较

9 I have ... / I've got ... 

## 过去时

10 was/were 

11 worked/got/went 等 (一般过去时)

12 I didn't ... Did you ...? (一般过去时的否定式与疑问式)

13 I was doing (过去进行时)

14 I was doing (过去进行时) 与 I did (一般过去时) 比较

## 现在完成时

15 I have done (现在完成时 1)

16 I've just ... I've already ... I haven't ... yet (现在完成时 2)

17 Have you ever ...? (现在完成时 3)

18 How long have you ...? (现在完成时 4)

19 for since ago 

20 I have done (现在完成时) 与 I did (一般过去时) 比较

```txt
36 I used to ...
```

there 与 it

48 How long does it take ...?

## 出版说明

剑桥“英语在用”（English in Use）丛书原由剑桥大学出版社出版，是一套享誉全球的英语学习用书，主要包括英语词汇、短语、习语、惯用搭配和语法等系列，自出版以来，全球销量已逾千万册，既可用于读者自学，也可用于课堂教学，是许多学习者手边必备的参考书。

剑桥“英语在用”丛书专为非英语国家的学习者编写，作者均为剑桥大学出版社卓有经验的权威，内容实例取材于剑桥国际英语语料库，在编排结构上条理明晰，形式简约，重点突出，注重实用；并采取版面左手页讲解、右手页练习，书后附参考答案的方式，达到即学即练的巩固效果。

自2001年以来，外语教学与研究出版社从剑桥大学出版社陆续引进了“英语在用”丛书的词汇、语法系列的学习用书及练习册，深受英语学习者和一些培训学校的青睐和好评。近来剑桥大学出版社重新修订、扩充了丛书内容，并推出了新的版本。鉴于“英语在用”丛书在学习者中的口碑和良好的学习效果，外语教学与研究出版社新引进了“英语在用”丛书的词汇、语法系列的修订新版以及此前未引进的系列（短语、习语等），特此推介给广大的读者，同时稍微更改了纸型和版式，使之更便于阅读。希望读者朋友们通过这套高品质的学习丛书，真正提高自己的英语水平。

For their help in producing this third edition of Essential Grammar in Use, I would like to thank Liz Driscoll, Jessica Roberts and Alison Sharpe. I would also like to thank the teachers and reviewers from various countries who provided me with feedback on the previous edition.

Design by Kamae Design 

## 致学生

本书是专为初级英语学习者设计的语法书，共由115个单元组成，每个单元分别论述一个语法点。“目录”中列出了各单元所含内容。

本书不必从头到尾依次学习，最好依需要而行。例如，对现在完成时（I have been, he has done 等）有疑问，可用“索引”（书后）找出相关单元（Units 15–20），随后进行与现在完成时相关的各个语法点的学习。

## 目录

如不确定从哪一个单元开始学习，可参看书后的“学习指导”。

Thanks ix  
致学生 x  
致老师 xii

现在时
1 am/is/are
2 am/is/are (疑问句)
3 I am doing (现在进行时)
4 are you doing? (现在进行时的疑问式)
5 I do/work/like 等 (一般现在时)
6 I don't ... (一般现在时的否定式)
7 Do you ...? (一般现在时的疑问式)
8 I am doing (现在进行时) 与 I do (一般现在时) 比较
9 I have ... / I've got ...

IF YOU ARE NOT SURE WHICH IS RIGHT
1.14 Please be quiet.
A I working. B I work. C I'm working. D I'm work.
1.15 Tom ____ a shower every morning.
A has. B having C is having D have
1.16 What at the weekend?
A do you usually B are you usually doing. C are you usually do
D do you usually do E you do usually
1.17 Sarah isn't feeling well. A headache.
A She have B She have got C She has D She's got
1.18 Tracey and Jeff ____ any children.
A don't have B doesn't have C no have D haven't got E haven't got
一般过去时
2.1 The weather ____ last week.
A is good B was good C were good D good E had good
2.2 Why ____ late this morning?
A you was B did you C was you D you were E were you
2.3 Terry ____ in a bank from 1996 to 2003.
A work B working C works D worked E was work
2.4 Caroline ____ to the cinema three times last week.
A go B went C goes D got E was
2.5 I ____ television yesterday.
A didn't watch B didn't watched C wasn't watched D don't watch
E didn't watching
2.6 'How ____? I don't know I didn't see it.'
A happened the accident B did happen the accident
C does the accident happen D did the accident happen
E the accident happened
2.7 What at 11.30 yesterday?
A were you doing B was you doing C you were doing D were you do
E you was doing.
2.8 Jack was reading a book when the phone ____
A ringing. B ring C rang D was ringing E was ring
2.9 I saw Lucy and Steve this morning. They ____ at the box stop.
A waiting. B waited C were waiting D was waiting E were waited
现在完成时
3.1 'Where's Rebecca' ____ to bed?
A She is gone B She has gone C She goes D She have gone
E She's gone
3.2 'Are Duase and Paul here?' 'No, they'
A don't arrive yet B have already arrived C haven't already arrived
D haven't arrived yet每单元分为两页：左手页为语法知识，右手页为练习。

## 语法知识

可依下列方式使用本书：

1. 从 “目录” 或 “索引” 处找出相关单元。

2. 学习左手页内容。

3. 做右手页练习。

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/e67fcddcebc80b87.jpg)


4. 参看第 284–310 页的“练习答案”核查答案。

5. 如有必要，再学一次左手页内容。

别忘了书后第244-252页的7个附录，此部分给出了主动语态与被动语态比较、不规则动词、缩略形式、拼写与短语动词等方面的内容。

书后第253-271页还有“补充练习”。第253页页端列出了这些练习的内容。

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/7d5b55522529554b.jpg)


## 致老师

## 特色

□主要针对语法，而非泛泛而谈。

□专为初级学习者设计，不涉及其他级别的内容。

□ 参考与练习相辅相成，融汇于同一册之中。

□既可供自学也可供教学使用。

## 组织结构

全书共115个单元，每一单元集中讲述一个语法点。材料依语法类别如时态、疑问句与冠词等划分，不依难易程度排序，因此可酌情自行选择。学习时不应从头学到尾。“目录”处列明内容，书后“索引”详尽。

每一单元设计相同：左手页讲述语法点，相应的练习则在右手页。第244-252页为7个附录，主要涉及主动语态与被动语态比较、不规则动词、缩略形式、拼写与短语动词等。老师如正确引导学生根据自己的程度利用这种编排结构灵活安排自己的学习进度，将会使其大有所获。

第 253-271 页为 “补充练习” 部分。这些练习为混合型，即将几个单元中的语法点（主要是与动词形式有关的语法点）糅合在一起。此部分有 35 个练习，第 253 页详列此项内容。

第 272-283 页为 “学习指导”，帮助学生确定学习哪些单元。

第 284–310 页为 “练习答案”，供学生核查答案使用。

## 水平

本书专为初学者即没有学过多少英语的学习者使用，但不适用于零起点的学生。本书也适用于语法较为薄弱的中低级学习者，或者在基础语法某些方面掌握不够扎实的学习者。

解释是针对初学者的，因此尽量简单易懂。例句与练习中的词汇量也依这一水准严格控制，以便保证全书的适用性。

## 用途

本书可供自学用（参见“致学生”），也可作为教学辅助材料。不论何种方式，都起到了初级语法书的作用。

本书作教学材料时可用于即时巩固、课后复习或补充学习，可供全班学生或个别有需要的学生使用。

本书左手页内容（讲述和解释）主要为自学者设计，因此老师在教学时最好按照自己的方式讲述语法点并搭配课后练习，左手页内容供学生课后参考使用。

本书作课后复习和补充学习使用时，老师可引导学生进行相关单元的自学和练习。

## 《剑桥初级英语语法》第三版

本书为《剑桥初级英语语法》的最新版。该版与上一版的区别如下：

□ 本书带有全新插图。

□ 新增Unit 35，部分结构调整，单元顺序变动较大。

□ 解释、例句和练习部分有不少细微改动。

□“补充练习”部分新增2页内容。

□书后新增“学习指导”部分，供学习者确定学习哪些单元。

## am/is/are

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/b8949a9c48aabe70.jpg)


## 肯定式

<table><tr><td>I</td><td>am</td><td>(I&#x27;m)</td></tr><tr><td>he she it</td><td>is</td><td>(he&#x27;s)(she&#x27;s)(it&#x27;s)</td></tr><tr><td>we you they</td><td>are</td><td>(we&#x27;re)(you&#x27;re)(they&#x27;re)</td></tr></table>

<table><tr><td>I</td><td>am not</td><td>(I&#x27;m not)</td></tr><tr><td>he she it</td><td>is not</td><td>(he&#x27;s not 或 he isn&#x27;t)(she&#x27;s not 或 she isn&#x27;t)(it&#x27;s not 或 it isn&#x27;t)</td></tr><tr><td>we you they</td><td>are not</td><td>(we&#x27;re not 或 we aren&#x27;t)(you&#x27;re not 或 you aren&#x27;t)(they&#x27;re not 或 they aren&#x27;t)</td></tr></table>

## 缩略形式

## 缩略形式

□ I'm cold. Can you close the window, please?
□ I'm 32 years old. My sister is 29.
□ Steve is ill. He's in bed.
□ My brother is afraid of dogs.
□ It's ten o'clock. You're late again.
□ Ann and I are good friends.
□ Your keys are on the table. 

□ I'm tired, but I'm not hungry. 

Tom isn't interested in politics. He's interested in music. 

□ Jane isn't a teacher. She's a student. 

□ Those people aren't English. They're Australian. 

□ It's sunny today, but it isn't warm. 

## that's = that is there's = there is here's = here is

□ Thank you. That's very kind of you. 

□ Look! There's Chris. 

□ 'Here's your key.' 'Thank you.' 

I'm afraid of dogs.

## Exercises

## 1.1 写出缩略形式（she's / we aren't 等）。

1 she is ____ she's ____ 3 it is not ____ 5 I am not ____
2 they are ____ 4 that is ____ 6 you are not ____. 

## 1.2 填入 am, is 或 are。

1 The weather ____ nice today. 5 Look! There ____ Carol. 

2 I .... not rich. 

6 My brother and I ____ good tennis players. 

3 This bag .... heavy.
7 Emily .... at home. Her children .... at school. 

4 These bags .... heavy. 8 I .... a taxi driver. My sister .... a nurse. 

## 1.3 完成下列句子。

1 Steve is ill. He's in bed. 

2 I'm not hungry, but ....thirsty. 

3 Mr Thomas is a very old man. 98. 

4 These chairs aren't beautiful, but ____ comfortable. 

5 The weather is nice today. warm and sunny. 

6 '..... late.' 'No, I'm not. I'm early!' 

7 Catherine isn't at home. .... at work. 

8 '…… your coat.' 'Oh, thank you very much.' 

## 1.4 参看莉萨所用的句子（Unit 1A）。现在写写你自己的情况。

1 (name?) My 5 (favourite colour or colours?) 

2 (from?) I ____ 

3 (age?) I 6 (interested in ... ?) 

4 (job?) I

## am/is/are（疑问句）

## 肯定式

<table><tr><td>I</td><td>am</td></tr><tr><td>he she it</td><td>is</td></tr><tr><td>we you they</td><td>are</td></tr></table>

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/023667158b4926b3.jpg)


<table><tr><td>am</td><td>I?</td></tr><tr><td>is</td><td>he?she?</td></tr><tr><td>are</td><td>we?you?they?</td></tr></table>

□ 'Am I late?' 'No, you're on time.' 

□ 'Is your mother at home?' 'No, she's out.' 

□ 'Are your parents at home?' 'No, they're out.' 

□ 'Is it cold in your room?' 'Yes, a little.' 

□ Your shoes are nice. Are they new? 

## 可以说：

□ Is she at home? / Is your mother at home? (而不用 Is at home your mother?)
□ Are they new? / Are your shoes new? (而不用 Are new your shoes?)

## Where ... ? / What ... ? / Who ... ? / How ... ? / Why ... ?

- Where is your mother? Is she at home?
- 'Where are you from?' 'Canada.'
- 'What colour is your car?' 'It's red.'
- 'How old is Joe?' 'He's 24.'
- How are your parents? Are they well?
- These postcards are nice. How much are they?
- This hotel isn't very good. Why is it so expensive? 

what's = what is who's = who is how's = how is where's = where is
□ What's the time? □ Who's that man?
□ Where's Lucy? □ How's your father? 

## 简略答语

<table><tr><td rowspan="3">Yes,</td><td>I</td><td>am.</td></tr><tr><td>hesheit</td><td>is.</td></tr><tr><td>weyouthey</td><td>are.</td></tr></table>

<table><tr><td rowspan="3">No,</td><td>I&#x27;m</td><td rowspan="3">not.</td></tr><tr><td>he&#x27;sshe&#x27;sit&#x27;s</td></tr><tr><td>we&#x27;reyou&#x27;rethey&#x27;re</td></tr></table>

<table><tr><td rowspan="2">No,</td><td>hesheit</td><td rowspan="2">isn&#x27;t.aren&#x27;t.</td></tr><tr><td>weyouthey</td></tr></table>

□ 'Are you tired?' 'Yes, I am.' 

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/7cd46f174a7b2528.jpg)


□ 'Are you hungry?' 'No, I'm not, but I'm thirsty.' 

□ 'Is your friend English?' 'Yes, he is.' 

□ 'Are these your keys?' 'Yes, they are.' 

□ 'That's my seat.' 'No, it isn't.'

## I am doing（现在进行时）

I'm eating. 

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/9ed42341dd2f8b9e.jpg)


She's eating.  
She isn't reading. 

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/52e3447ed6f067ec.jpg)


It's raining.  
The sun isn't shining. 

We're running. 

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/3022cdf5438332ad.jpg)



They're running.  
They aren't walking.


现在进行时的形式为：

am/is/are + doing/eating/running/writing 等。

<table><tr><td>I</td><td>am (not)</td><td rowspan="3">-ing</td></tr><tr><td>he she it</td><td>is (not)</td></tr><tr><td>we you they</td><td>are (not)</td></tr></table>

□ I'm working. I'm not watching TV. 

□ Maria is reading a newspaper. 

□ She isn't eating. (或 She's not eating.)

□ The phone is ringing. 

□ We're having dinner. 

□ You're not listening to me. (或 You aren't listening ...)

☐ The children are doing their homework. 

am/is/are + -ing 表示 “现在正在发生某事”：

I'm working 

she's wearing a hat 

they're playing football 

I'm not watching television 

过去

现在

将来

□ Please be quiet. I'm working. (= I'm working now) 

□ Look, there's Sarah. She's wearing a brown coat. (= she is wearing it now) 

□ The weather is nice. It's not raining. 

□ 'Where are the children?' 'They're playing in the park.' 

□ (on the phone) We're having dinner now. Can I phone you later? 

□ You can turn off the television. I'm not watching it. 

拼写（参见附录5）：

come → coming 

write → writing 

run → running 

dance → dancing 

sit → sitting 

swim → swimming 

lie → lying 

am/is/are → Unit 1 are you doing? (疑问式) → Unit 4 I am doing 与 I do 比较 → Unit 8 What are you doing tomorrow? → Unit 25

## are you doing? (现在进行时的疑问式)

## 肯定式

<table><tr><td>I</td><td>am</td><td rowspan="3">doing working going staying等</td></tr><tr><td>he she it</td><td>is</td></tr><tr><td>we you they</td><td>are</td></tr></table>

## 疑问式

<table><tr><td>am</td><td>I</td><td rowspan="3">doing?working?going?staying?等</td></tr><tr><td>is</td><td>hesheit</td></tr><tr><td>are</td><td>weyouthey</td></tr></table>

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/a1f9ccd8b3706206.jpg)


□ 'Are you feeling OK?' 'Yes, I'm fine, thanks.' 

□ 'Is it raining?' 'Yes, take an umbrella.' 

□ Why are you wearing a coat? It's not cold. 

□ 'What's Paul doing?' 'He's reading the newspaper.' 

□ 'What are the children doing?' 'They're watching television.' 

□ Look, there's Emily! Where's she going? 

□ Who are you waiting for? Are you waiting for Sue? 

## 请看现在进行时疑问式的词序：

is/are + 主语 + -ing

<table><tr><td>WhereWhere</td><td>IsIsareare</td><td>hePaultheythose people</td><td>working today?working today?(而不用 Is working Paul today?)going?going?(而不用 Where are going those people?)</td></tr></table>

## 简略答语

<table><tr><td rowspan="3">Yes,</td><td>I</td><td>am.</td><td rowspan="3">No,</td><td>I&#x27;m</td><td rowspan="3">not.</td><td rowspan="3">或</td><td rowspan="3">No,</td><td rowspan="2">hesheit</td><td rowspan="2">isn&#x27;t.</td></tr><tr><td>hesheit</td><td>is.</td><td>he&#x27;sShe&#x27;sit&#x27;s</td></tr><tr><td>weyouthey</td><td>are.</td><td>we&#x27;reyou&#x27;rethey&#x27;re</td><td>weyouthey</td><td>aren&#x27;t.</td></tr></table>


□ 'Are you going now?' 'Yes, I am.' 



□ 'Is Paul working today?' 'Yes, he is.' 



□ 'Is it raining?' 'No, it isn't.' 



□ 'Are your friends staying at a hotel?' 'No, they aren't. They're staying with me.'

## 4.3 将下列词语正确排序，组成问句。

1 (is / working / Paul / today) Is Paul working today
2 (what / the children / are / doing) What are the children doing
3 (you / are / listening / to me)
4 (where / your friends / are / going)
5 (are / watching / your parents / television)
6 (what / Jessica / is / cooking)
7 (why / you / are / looking / at me)
8 (is / coming / the bus)

1 Are you watching TV? No, I'm not. 4 Is it raining?

## I do/work/like 等（一般现在时）

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/2387db552bb6373f.jpg)


They're looking at their books. They read a lot. 

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/0dacb1c023bd0e4b.jpg)


He's eating an ice-cream. He likes ice-cream. 

they read / he likes / I work 等为一般现在时：

<table><tr><td>I/we/you/they</td><td>read</td><td>like</td><td>work</td><td>live</td><td>watch</td><td>do</td><td>have</td></tr><tr><td>he/she/it</td><td>reads</td><td>likes</td><td>works</td><td>lives</td><td>watches</td><td>does</td><td>has</td></tr></table>

he works / she lives / it rains 等:
☐ I work in a shop. My brother works in a bank. (而不用 My brother work)
☐ Lucy lives in London. Her parents live in Scotland.
☐ It rains a lot in winter.
I have → he/she/it has:

I have → he/she/it has:
□ John has a shower every day. 

拼写（参见附录5）：

-es 用于 -s / -sh / -ch 之后： pass → passes finish → finishes watch → watches
-y → -ies: study → studies try → tries
还有： do → does go → goes

一般现在时可用来表示一般性的事实、有时或经常发生的事情：
□ I like big cities.
□ Your English is good. You speak very well.
□ Tim works very hard. He starts at 7.30 and finishes at 8 o'clock in the evening.
□ The earth goes round the sun.
□ We do a lot of different things in our free time.
□ It costs a lot of money to build a hospital.

always/never/often/usually/sometimes 常与一般现在时连用：
□ Sue always gets to work early. (而不用 Sue gets always)
□ I never eat breakfast. (而不用 I eat never)
□ We often go away at weekends.
□ Mark usually plays football on Sundays.
□ I sometimes walk to work, but not very often.

I don't ...（否定式）→ Unit 6 Do you ...? （疑问式）→ Unit 7 I am doing 与 I do 比较 → Unit 8 always/usually/often 等（词序）→ Unit 94

# I don't ... (一般现在时的否定式)

## 一般现在时的否定式为 don't/doesn't + 动词：

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/3f3da5526a15b560.jpg)


She doesn't drink coffee. 

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/6936d0c9d36144bf.jpg)



He doesn't like his job.


## 肯定式

否定式

<table><tr><td>Iweyouthey</td><td>worklikedohave</td><td>Iweyouthey</td><td>don&#x27;t(do not)</td><td rowspan="2">worklikedo have</td></tr><tr><td>hesheit</td><td>workslikesdoeshas</td><td>hesheit</td><td>doesn&#x27;t(does not)</td></tr></table>

□ I drink coffee, but I don't drink tea. 

□ Sue drinks tea, but she doesn't drink coffee. 

□ You don't work very hard. 

□ We don't watch television very often. 

□ The weather is usually nice. It doesn't rain very often. 

□ Gary and Nicole don't know many people. 

## 记住：

I/we/you/they don't ... □ I don't like football.
he/she/it doesn't ... □ He doesn't like football. 

□ I don't like Fred and Fred doesn't like me. (而不用 Fred don't like)

□ My car doesn't use much petrol. (而不用 My car don't use)

□ Sometimes he is late, but it doesn't happen very often. 

要用 don't/doesn't + 动词原形 (don't like / doesn't speak / doesn't do 等，而不用其他形式):

□ I don't like washing the car. I don't do it very often. 

□ Sarah speaks Spanish, but she doesn't speak Italian. (而不用 doesn't speaks)

□ Bill doesn't do his job very well. (而不用 Bill doesn't his job)

□ Paula doesn't usually have breakfast. (而不用 doesn't ... has)

# Do you ... ? (一般现在时的疑问式)

## 一般现在时的疑问式中用 do/does:

<table><tr><td>Iweyouthey</td><td>worklikedohave</td></tr><tr><td>hesheit</td><td>workslikesdoeshas</td></tr></table>

疑问式

<table><tr><td>do</td><td>Iweyouthey</td><td rowspan="2">work?like?do?have?</td></tr><tr><td>does</td><td>hesheit</td></tr></table>

Do you play the guitar? 

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/097d7e5ee6a30a19.jpg)


## 请看一般现在时疑问式的词序：

## do/does + 主语 + 动词原形

<table><tr><td>WhereHow oftenWhatHow much</td><td>DoDoDoesdo doesdoes</td><td>youyour friendsChrisyour parents youthis wordit</td><td>workliveplaylive?washmean?cost</td><td>on Sundays?near here?tennis?your hair?to fly to Rome?</td></tr></table>

## 带 always/usually/often 的疑问句：

<table><tr><td>What</td><td>Do Does do</td><td>you Chris you</td><td>always often usually</td><td>have phone do</td><td>breakfast? you? at weekends?</td></tr></table>

What do you do? 表示 “你是做什么工作的”：
□ ‘What do you do?’ ‘I work in a bank.’

## 记住：

## 简略答语

<table><tr><td>I/we/you/they do.</td></tr><tr><td>he/she/it does.</td></tr></table>

<table><tr><td rowspan="2">No,</td><td>I/we/you/they don&#x27;t.</td></tr><tr><td>he/she/it doesn&#x27;t.</td></tr></table>

□ 'Do you play tennis?' 'No, I don't.' 

□ 'Do your parents speak English?' 'Yes, they do.' 

□ 'Does Gary work hard?' 'Yes, he does.' 

□ 'Does your sister live in London.' 'No, she doesn't.'

## 你可以说 I have 或 I've got, he has 或 he's got 等:

<table><tr><td>Iweyouthey</td><td>have</td><td rowspan="2">或</td><td>Iweyouthey</td><td>have got</td><td>(I’ve got)(we’ve got)(you’ve got)(they’ve got)</td></tr><tr><td>hesheit</td><td>has</td><td>hesheit</td><td>has got</td><td>(he’s got)(she’s got)(it’s got)</td></tr></table>

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/3d207e94d1d88247.jpg)


□ I have blue eyes. 或 I've got blue eyes.

□ Tim has two sisters. 或 Tim has got two sisters.

□ Our car has four doors. 或 Our car has got four doors.

□ Sarah isn't feeling well. She has a headache. 或 She's got a headache.

□ They like animals. They have a horse, three dogs and six cats. 或 They've got a horse ...

## I haven't got / have you got? 等

<table><tr><td>Iweyouthey</td><td>have not(haven’t)</td><td rowspan="2">got</td><td>have</td><td>Iweyouthey</td><td rowspan="2">got?</td><td>Yes,No,</td><td>Iweyouthey</td><td rowspan="2">have.haven’t.has.hasn’t.</td></tr><tr><td>hesheit</td><td>has not(hasn’t)</td><td>has</td><td>hesheit</td><td>Yes,No,</td><td>hesheit</td></tr></table>

□ I've got a motorbike, but I haven't got a car. 

□ Tracey and Jeff haven't got any children. 

□ It's a nice house, but it hasn't got a garden. 

□ 'Have you got a camera?' 'No, I haven't.' 

□ 'What have you got in your bag?' 'Nothing. It's empty.' 

□ 'Has Helen got a car?' 'Yes, she has.' 

□ What kind of car has she got? 

## I don't have / do you have? 等

否定式与疑问式中也可以用 do/does:

□ They don't have any children. (= They haven't got any children.) 

□ It's a nice house, but it doesn't have a garden. (= it hasn't got a garden) 

□ Does Helen have a car? (= Has Helen got a car?) 

□ What do you have in your bag? (= What have you got in your bag?) 

had / didn't have（一般过去时）→ Units 11-12 have breakfast / have a shower 等 → Unit 58 some/any → Unit 76

## last night

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/2532248f7f534bb0.jpg)



Now Robert is at work.



At midnight last night he wasn't at work.



He was in bed.
He was asleep.


am/is (现在) → was (过去):

□ I am tired (now). 

□ Where is Kate (now)? 

□ The weather is good today. 

I was tired last night.
Where was Kate yesterday?
The weather was good last week. 

are (现在) → were (过去):

□ You are late (now). 

□ They aren't here (now). 

You were late yesterday. They weren't here last Sunday. 

## 肯定式

<table><tr><td>I he she it</td><td>was</td></tr><tr><td>we you they</td><td>were</td></tr></table>

<table><tr><td>I he she it</td><td>was not (wasn&#x27;t)</td></tr><tr><td>we you they</td><td>were not (weren&#x27;t)</td></tr></table>

疑问式

<table><tr><td>was</td><td>I?he?she?it?</td></tr><tr><td>were</td><td>we?you?they?</td></tr></table>

□ Last year Rachel was 22, so she is 23 now. 

□ When I was a child, I was afraid of dogs. 

□ We were hungry after the journey, but we weren't tired. 

☐ The hotel was comfortable, but it wasn't expensive. 

□ Was the weather nice when you were on holiday? 

□ Your shoes are nice. Were they expensive? 

□ Why were you late this morning? 

## 简略答语

<table><tr><td rowspan="2">Yes,</td><td>I/he/she/it was.</td></tr><tr><td>we/you/they were.</td></tr></table>

<table><tr><td rowspan="2">No,</td><td>I/he/she/it wasn&#x27;t.</td></tr><tr><td>we/you/they weren&#x27;t.</td></tr></table>

□ 'Were you late?' 'No, I wasn't.' 

□ 'Was Ted at work yesterday?' 'Yes, he was.' 

□ 'Were Sue and Steve at the party?' 'No, they weren't.' 

SUE 

BEN

## 10.2 填入 am/is/are（现在时）或 was/were（过去时）。

1 Last year she was 22, so she is 23 now.

4 I feel fine this morning, but I ____ very tired last night. 

5 Where you at 11 o'clock last Friday morning? 

6 Don't buy those shoes. They ____ very expensive. 

7 I like your new jacket. ____ it expensive? 

8 This time last year I .... in Paris.

watched 为 watch 的过去式:

<table><tr><td>I/we/you/they he/she/it</td><td>watched</td></tr></table>

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/342885e099a60c2f.jpg)


## 过去式通常为 -ed 形式（指规则动词）。例如：

work → worked dance → danced 

clean → cleaned    stay → stayed 

start → started need → needed 

□ I clean my teeth every morning. This morning I cleaned my teeth. 

□ Terry worked in a bank from 1996 to 2003. 

□ Yesterday it rained all morning. It stopped at lunchtime. 

☐ We enjoyed the party last night. We danced a lot and talked to a lot of people. The party finished at midnight. 

拼写（参见附录5）：

try → tried study → studied copy → copied 

stop → stopped 

plan → planned 

有些动词为不规则动词，它们的过去式不是 -ed 形式。下表列出了一些重要的不规则动词及其过去式（更多信息参见附录 2-3）：

<table><tr><td colspan="2">begin → began</td><td colspan="2">fall → fell</td><td colspan="2">leave → left</td><td colspan="2">sell → sold</td></tr><tr><td>break</td><td>broke</td><td>find</td><td>found</td><td>lose</td><td>lost</td><td>sit</td><td>sat</td></tr><tr><td>bring</td><td>brought</td><td>fly</td><td>flew</td><td>make</td><td>made</td><td>sleep</td><td>slept</td></tr><tr><td>build</td><td>built</td><td>forget</td><td>forgot</td><td>meet</td><td>met</td><td>speak</td><td>spoke</td></tr><tr><td>buy</td><td>bought</td><td>get</td><td>got</td><td>pay</td><td>paid</td><td>stand</td><td>stood</td></tr><tr><td>catch</td><td>caught</td><td>give</td><td>gave</td><td>put</td><td>put</td><td>take</td><td>took</td></tr><tr><td>come</td><td>came</td><td>go</td><td>went</td><td>read</td><td>read (red)*</td><td>tell</td><td>told</td></tr><tr><td>do</td><td>did</td><td>have</td><td>had</td><td>ring</td><td>rang</td><td>think</td><td>thought</td></tr><tr><td>drink</td><td>drank</td><td>hear</td><td>heard</td><td>say</td><td>said</td><td>win</td><td>won</td></tr><tr><td>eat</td><td>ate</td><td>know</td><td>knew</td><td>see</td><td>saw</td><td>write</td><td>wrote</td></tr></table>

## I didn't ... Did you ... ?

## (一般过去时的否定式与疑问式)

## A 一般过去时的否定式与疑问式中用 did:

## 动词原形 肯定式

<table><tr><td>playstartwatchhaveseedoogo</td><td>Iweyoutheyhesheit</td><td>playedstartedwatchedhadsawsdidwent</td><td>Iweyoutheyhesheit</td><td>did not(didn’t)</td><td>playstartwatchhaveseedogo</td><td>did</td><td>Iweyoutheyhesheit</td><td>play?start?watch?have?see?do?go?</td></tr></table>

## do/does (现在) → did (过去):

□ I don't watch television very often. 

I didn't watch television yesterday. 

□ Does she often go away? 

Did she go away last week? 

## 要用 did/didn't + 动词原形 (watch/play/go 等):

<table><tr><td>I watchedthey wenthe hadyou did</td><td>但用 I didn&#x27;t watchdid they go?he didn&#x27;t havedid you do?</td><td>(而不用 I didn&#x27;t watched)(而不用 did they went?)</td></tr></table>

□ I played tennis yesterday, but I didn't win. 

□ 'Did you do the shopping?' 'No, I didn't have time.' 

□ We went to the cinema, but we didn't enjoy the film. 

请看一般过去时疑问式的词序：

did + 主语 + 动词原形

<table><tr><td>What How Where</td><td>Did did did did</td><td>your sister you the accident your parents</td><td>phone do happen? go</td><td>you? last night? for their holiday?</td></tr></table>

## 简略答语

<table><tr><td>Yes,</td><td>I/we/you/they he/she/it</td><td>did.</td><td>No,</td><td>I/we/you/they he/she/it</td><td>didn&#x27;t.</td></tr></table>

□ 'Did you see Joe yesterday?' 'No, I didn't.' 

□ 'Did it rain on Sunday?' 'Yes, it did.' 

□ 'Did Helen come to the party?' 'No, she didn't.' 

□ 'Did your parents have a good holiday?' 'Yes, they did.'

<table><tr><td colspan="2">arrive cost go go to bed late happen have a nice time stay win</td></tr><tr><td>1 A: We went to New York last month.B: Where did you stay.A: With some friends.</td><td>5 A: We came home by taxi.B: How much.A: Ten pounds.</td></tr><tr><td>2 A: I was late for the meeting.B: What time.A: Half past nine.</td><td>6 A: I&#x27;m tired this morning.B: A: No, but I didn&#x27;t sleep very well.</td></tr><tr><td>3 A: I played tennis this afternoon.B: A: No, I lost.</td><td>7 A: We went to the beach yesterday.B: A: Yes, it was great.</td></tr><tr><td>4 A: I had a nice holiday.B: Good. Where.A: To the mountains.</td><td>8 A: The window is broken.B: How.A: I don&#x27;t know.</td></tr></table>

1 We went to the cinema, but the film wasn't very good. We didn't enjoy it. (enjoy)

3 '____ yesterday?' 'No, it was a nice day.' (rain)

8 'Why weren't you at the meeting yesterday?' 'I ____ about it.' (know)

was/were + -ing 为过去进行时结构：

肯定式

<table><tr><td>Ihesheit</td><td>was</td><td rowspan="2">doingwatchingplayingswimmingliving等</td><td>Ihesheit</td><td>was not(wasn’t)</td><td rowspan="2">doingwatchingplayingswimmingliving等</td><td>was</td><td>Ihesheit</td><td rowspan="2">doing?watching?playing?swimming?living?等</td></tr><tr><td>weyouthey</td><td>were</td><td>weyouthey</td><td>were not(weren’t)</td><td>were</td><td>weyouthey</td></tr></table>

□ What were you doing at 11.30 yesterday? Were you working?

□ Today she's wearing a skirt, but yesterday she was wearing trousers.

am/is/are + -ing (现在) → was/were + -ing (过去):

现在

过去

□ It wasn't raining when we went out.

## I was doing（过去进行时）与 I did（一般过去时）比较

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/3a5fa9832f3cb5ef.jpg)


Jack was reading a book. 

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/ab6a0be1d838c98a.jpg)



The phone rang.


![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/67e3af9f3ec77e37.jpg)



He stopped reading.


![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/5e7e93ec41a24432.jpg)



He answered the phone.


What happened? The phone rang. (一般过去时)

What was Jack doing when the phone rang? He was reading a book. (过去进行时)

What did he do when the phone rang?
He stopped reading and answered the phone. } (一般过去时)

杰克在电话铃响之前已开始看书，所以应说：When the phone rang, he was reading.

<table><tr><td>he started reading</td><td>the phone rang</td><td>he stopped reading</td><td>he answered the phone</td></tr><tr><td colspan="4">he was reading</td></tr></table>

## 一般过去时

☐ A: What did you do yesterday morning?
B: We played tennis (from 10 to 11.30). 

## 过去进行时

10 o'clock 

☐ A: What were you doing at 10.30?
B: We were playing tennis. 

结束
11.30开始

10 o'clock 

## we played (动作完成)

□ Jack read a book yesterday. (= from beginning to end) 

□ Did you watch the film on television last night? 

□ Jack was reading a book when the phone rang. 

□ It didn't rain while we were on holiday. 

□ Were you watching television when I phoned you? 

□ It wasn't raining when I got up. 

☐ I started work at 9 o'clock and finished at 4.30. At 2.30 I was working. 

☐ It was raining when we went out. (= it started raining before we went out) 

□ I saw Lucy and Steve this morning. They were waiting at the bus stop. 

□ Kelly fell asleep while she was reading.

14.2 用动词的过去进行时或一般过去时形式填空。

1 A: What were you doing (you/do) when the phone rang (ring)?  
B: I was watching (watch) television. 

2 A: Was Jane busy when you went to see her?
B: Yes, she ____ (study). 

3 A: What time (the post / arrive) this morning?
B: It (come) while I (have) breakfast. 

4 A: Was Tracey at work today?
B: No, she ____ (not/go) to work. She was ill. 

5 A: How fast (you/drive) when the police stop?  
B: I'm not sure, but I (not/drive) very fast. 

7 A: How ____ (you/break) the window? 

B: We ____ (play) football. I ____ (kick) the ball and it ____ (hit) the window. 

9 A: What ____ (you/do) at 2 o'clock this morning?
B: I was asleep. 

10 A: I (lose) my key last night.  
B: How (you/get) into your room?  
A: I (climb) in through a window. 

## Unit 15

## I have done (现在完成时 1)

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/d03f44c9e7648848.jpg)



His shoes are dirty.


![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/38a5c1a5ae08b152.jpg)



He is cleaning his shoes.


![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/008c0d300f37b6c2.jpg)


He has cleaned his shoes. (= his shoes are clean now) 

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/26635f1b3476ef49.jpg)


They are at home. 

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/72d3011c4ce8c464.jpg)



They are going out.


![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/f6b5aa0b3baab870.jpg)



They have gone out.
(= they are not at home now)


## has cleaned / have gone 等为现在完成时结构 (have + 过去分词):

<table><tr><td>Iweyouthey</td><td>have(&#x27;ve)have not(haven&#x27;t)</td><td rowspan="2">cleanedfinishedstartedlostdonebeengone</td><td>have</td><td>Iweyouthey</td><td rowspan="2">cleaned?finished?started?lost?done?been?gone?</td><td rowspan="2">规则动词不规则动词</td></tr><tr><td>hesheit</td><td>has(&#x27;s)has not(hasn&#x27;t)</td><td>has</td><td>hesheit</td></tr></table>

## 过去分词

规则动词的过去分词为 -ed 形式 (与过去式相同):

```txt
clean → I have cleaned finish → we have finished start → she has started 
```

不规则动词的过去分词不是 -ed 形式。

有些与过去式相同：

```txt
buy → I bought / I have bought have → he had / he has had 
```

有些与过去式不同：

```txt
现在完成时表示发生在过去而又对现在产生某种影响的动作：
□ I've lost my passport. (= I can't find my passport now)
□ 'Where's Rebecca?' 'She's gone to bed.' (= she is in bed now)
□ We've bought a new car. (= we have a new car now)
□ It's Rachel's birthday tomorrow and I haven't bought her a present. (= I don't have a present for her now)
□ 'Bob is away on holiday.' 'Oh, where has he gone?' (= where is he now?)
□ Can I take this newspaper? Have you finished with it? (= do you need it now?)
现在完成时 → Units 16-19 现在完成时与一般过去时比较 → Unit 20 不规则动词 → Unit 24，附录 2-3
```

15.1 根据图片内容，用下列短语造句。

go to bed clean his shoes stop raining close the door fall down have a shower 

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/a8589383ac819bd1.jpg)


## 15.2 用方框中的动词完成句子。

<table><tr><td>break</td><td>buy</td><td>decide</td><td>finish</td><td>forget</td><td>go</td><td>go</td></tr><tr><td>invite</td><td>read</td><td>see</td><td>not/see</td><td>take</td><td>tell</td><td>not/tell</td></tr></table>

1 'Can I have a look at your newspaper?' 'Yes, I've finished with it.' 

2 I .... some new shoes. Do you want to see them? 

3 'Where is Liz?' 'She's not here. She .... out.' 

4 I'm looking for Paula. ____ you ____ her? 

5 Look! Somebody ____ that window. 

6 'Does Lisa know that you're going away?' 'Yes, I ____ her.' 

7 I can't find my umbrella. Somebody it. 

8 'Where are my glasses?' 'I don't know. I ____ them.' 

9 I'm looking for Sarah. Where ____ she ____? 

10 I know that woman, but I ____ her name. 

11 Sue is having a party tonight. She ____ a lot of people. 

12 What are you going to do? ____ you ____? 

13 A: Does Bill know about the meeting tomorrow? 

B: I don't think so. I ____ him. 

14 'Do you want this magazine?' 'No, I it, thanks.' 

## Unit 16

## I've just ... I've already ... I haven't ... yet (现在完成时 2)

## I've just ...

just 表示 “刚才”：
□ A: Are Diane and Paul here?
B: Yes, they've just arrived.

□ A: Are you hungry?
B: No, I've just had dinner. 

□ A: Is Tom here?
B: No, I'm afraid he's just gone.
(= he has just gone) 

## I've already ...

already 表示 “已经”（在你 / 我预料到之前）：

□ A: What time are Diane and Paul coming? 

B: They've already arrived. (= before you expected) 

□ It's only 9 o'clock and Anna has already gone to bed. (= before I expected) 

□ A: Jon, this is Emma. 

B: Yes, I know. We've already met. 

yet 表示 “直到现在”。

## I haven't ... yet / Have you ... yet?

yet 用于否定句与疑问句中，通常出现在句尾。

Yes, I know. We've already met. 

yet 用于否定句中 (I haven't ... yet):

B: No, they haven't arrived yet.
(但B期望黛安娜与保罗很快到达)

□ A: Are Diane and Paul here? 

□ A: Does James know that you're going away? 

B: No, I haven't told him yet.
(但B很快就会告诉他)

yet 用于疑问句中 (Have you ... yet?):

□ Silvia has bought a new dress, but she hasn't worn it yet. 

□ A: Have Diane and Paul arrived yet? 

B: No, not yet. We're still waiting for them. 

□ A: Has Nicole started her new job yet? 

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/4ae43b33bff2f25e.jpg)



They have just arrived.


B: No, she starts next week. 

□ A: This is my new dress. 

B: Oh, it's nice. Have you worn it yet? 

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/9f84bfe9b0c138df.jpg)


![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/7f049e782906be51.jpg)


The film hasn't started yet. 

This is my new dress. 

Oh, it's nice. Have you worn it yet? 

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/bf5cfc4e584d5dcb.jpg)

1 Your friend has got a new job. Perhaps she has started it. You ask her: Have you started your new job yet?

## Have you ever ... ? (现在完成时 3)

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/de12ddf700b639ac.jpg)


Have you ever been to Japan? 

现在完成时 (have been / have had / have played 等) 可用来谈论从过去到现在的一段时间，如一个人的一生：

## Have you ever been to Japan?

过去

现在

□ 'Have you been to France?' 'No, I haven't.' 

□ I've been to Canada, but I haven't been to the United States. 

Mary is an interesting person. She has had many different jobs and has lived in many places. 

□ I've seen that woman before, but I can't remember where. 

□ How many times has Brazil won the World Cup? 

□ 'Have you read this book?' 'Yes, I've read it twice.' (twice 表示 “两次”)

## 现在完成时与 ever (用于疑问句中) / never 连用：

□ 'Has Ann ever been to Australia?' 'Yes, once.' (once 表示 “一次”)

□ 'Have you ever played golf?' 'Yes, I play a lot.' 

□ My sister has never travelled by plane. 

□ I've never ridden a horse. 

□ 'Who is that man?' 'I don't know. I've never seen him before.' 

## gone 与 been 比较：

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/0dfd971080dfe194.jpg)


## 请比较：

□ I can't find Susan. Where has she gone? (= where is she now?) 

□ Oh, hello Susan! I was looking for you. Where have you been?

## for since ago

for 与 since 比较

for 与 since 可用来表示多久：

□ Jane is in Ireland. She has been there 

for + 一段时间 (three days / two years 等):

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/37c826dd8cbaa0b4.jpg)


过去


现在

☐ Richard has been in Canada for six months. (而不用 since six months)

□ We've been waiting for two hours. (而不用 since two hours)

□ I've lived in London for a long time. 

for three days.
since Monday. 

since + 一段时间的起点 (Monday / 9 o'clock 等):

<table><tr><td colspan="2">起点</td></tr><tr><td>Monday</td><td>since Monday</td></tr></table>

过去

现在

<table><tr><td colspan="2">since</td></tr><tr><td>Monday</td><td>Wednesday</td></tr><tr><td>9 o&#x27;clock</td><td>12.30</td></tr><tr><td>24 July</td><td>Christmas</td></tr><tr><td>January</td><td>I was ten years old</td></tr><tr><td>1985</td><td>we arrived</td></tr></table>

☐ Richard has been in Canada since January. (= from January to now) 

□ We've been waiting since 9 o'clock. (= from 9 o'clock to now) 

□ I've lived in London since I was ten years old. 

## ago

ago 表示 “之前，以前”：

□ Susan started her new job three weeks ago. (= three weeks before now) 

□ 'When did Tom go out?' 'Ten minutes ago.' (= ten minutes before now) 

□ I had dinner an hour ago. 

□ Life was very different a hundred years ago. 

ago 与动词的过去式 (started/did/had/was 等) 连用。

请比较 ago 与 for:

□ When did Jane arrive in Ireland?
She arrived in Ireland three days ago. 

□ How long has she been in Ireland? She has been in Ireland for three days. 

## Exercises

19.1 用 for 或 since 填空。
1 Jane has been in Ireland ____ since ____ Monday.
2 Jane has been in Ireland ____ for ____ three days.
3 My aunt has lived in Australia ____ 15 years.
4 Jennifer is in her office. She has been there ____ 7 o'clock.
5 India has been an independent country ____ 1947.
6 The bus is late. We've been waiting ____ 20 minutes.
7 Nobody lives in those houses. They have been empty ____ many years.
8 Michael has been ill ____ a long time. He has been in hospital ____ October.
19.2 用 ago 回答下列问题。
1 When was your last meal? Three hours ago.
2 When was the last time you were ill?
3 When did you last go to the cinema?
4 When was the last time you were in a car?
5 When was the last time you went on holiday?
19.3 用括号中的词语和 for 或 ago 完成句子。
1 Jane arrived in Ireland ____ three days ago. (three days)
2 Jane has been in Ireland ____ for three days. (three days)
3 Lynn and Mark have been married ____ (20 years)
4 Lynn and Mark got married ____ (20 years)
5 Dan arrived ____ (an hour)
6 I bought these shoes ____ (a few days)
7 Silvia has been learning English ____ (six months)
8 Have you known Lisa ____ ? (a long time)
19.4 用 for 或 since 完成句子。
1 (Jane is in Ireland – she arrived there three days ago) Jane has been in Ireland for three days.
2 (Jack is here – he arrived on Tuesday) Jack has
3 (It's raining – it started an hour ago) It's been
4 (I know Sue – I first met her in 2002) I've
5 (Claire and Matthew are married – they got married six months ago) Claire and Matthew have
6 (Liz is studying medicine at university – she started three years ago) Liz has
7 (David plays the piano – he started when he was seven years old) David has
19.5 根据你自己的情况，用下列句式造句。

## I have done（现在完成时）与

## I did（一般过去时）比较

与动作完成的时间 (yesterday / last week 等) 连用时，用一般过去时 (arrived/saw/was 等):

一般过去时 + 动作完成的时间

<table><tr><td>We arrived</td><td>yesterday. last week. at 3 o&#x27;clock. in 2002. six months ago.</td><td>______</td><td>yesterday last week six months ago动作完成的时间</td></tr></table>

过去 现在

不要将现在完成时 (have arrived / have done / have been 等) 与动作完成的时间连用:

□ I saw Paula yesterday. (而不用 I have seen)

□ Where were you on Sunday afternoon? (而不用 Where have you been)

□ We didn't have a holiday last year. (而不用 We haven't had)

□ 'What did you do last night?' 'I stayed at home.' 

□ William Shakespeare lived from 1564 to 1616. He was a writer. He wrote many plays and poems. 

可用一般现在时询问 When ...? 或 What time ...? 类型的问题：

□ When did you buy your computer? (而不用 When have you bought)

□ What time did Andy go out? (而不用 What time has Andy gone out?)

## 请比较：

## 现在完成时

□ I have lost my key. 

(= I can't find it now) 

一般过去时

□ I lost my key last week. 

□ Ben has gone home. 

(= he isn't here now) 

□ Ben went home ten minutes ago. 

□ Have you seen Kate? 

(= where is she now?) 

□ Did you see Kate on Saturday? 

现在

现在

□ Have you ever been to Spain?
(= in your life, until now) 

□ My friend is a writer. He has written many books. 

□ The letter hasn't arrived yet. 

□ Did you go to Spain last year? 

□ We've lived in Singapore for six years. (= we live there now) 

□ Shakespeare wrote many plays and poems. 

□ The letter didn't arrive yesterday. 

□ We lived in Glasgow for six years, but now we live in Singapore.

## 20.3 用动词的现在完成时或一般过去时形式填空。

1 My friend is a writer. He ____ has written ____ (write) many books.
2 We ____ didn't have ____ (not/have) a holiday last year.
3 I ____ (play) tennis yesterday afternoon.
4 What time ____ (you/go) to bed last night?
5 ____ (you/ever/meet) a famous person?
6 The weather ____ (not/be) very good yesterday.
7 Kathy travels a lot. She ____ (visit) many countries.
8 I ____ (switch) off the light before going out this morning.
9 I live in New York now, but I ____ (live) in Mexico for many years.
10 'What's Canada like? Is it beautiful?' 'I don't know. I ____ (not/be) there.' 

## 20.4 用动词的现在完成时或一般过去时形式填空。

1 A: Have you ever been (you/ever/be) to Florida?
B: Yes, we went (go) there on holiday two years ago.
A: (you/have) a good time?
B: Yes, it (be) great. 

2 A: Where's Alan? (you/see) him?
B: Yes, he (go) out a few minutes ago.
A: And Rachel?
B: I don't know. I (not/see) her. 

3 Rose works in a factory. She ____ (work) there for six months.
Before that she ____ (be) a waitress in a restaurant. She ____ (work) there for two years, but she ____ (not/enjoy) it very much. 

4 A: Do you know Martin's sister?
B: I ____ (see) her a few times, but I ____ (never/speak) to her. ____ (you/ever/speak) to her?
A: Yes. I ____ (meet) her at a party last week. She's very nice. 

## → 补充练习 19-23，29-31（第261-263页，第266-268页）

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/c94adba592384048.jpg)


The office is cleaned every day. 

The office was cleaned yesterday. 

请比较主动语态与被动语态：

Somebody cleans the office every day. (主动)

The office is cleaned every day. （被动）

Somebody cleaned the office yesterday. （主动）

The office was cleaned yesterday. （被动）

## 被动语态

过去分词

<table><tr><td>am/is/arewas/were</td><td>(not)</td><td>+</td><td>cleanedinventedinjured</td><td>donebuilttaken等</td></tr></table>

规则动词的过去分词为 -ed 形式 (cleaned/damaged 等)。

关于不规则动词的过去分词形式 (done/built/taken 等)，参见附录 2-3。

□ Butter is made from milk. 

□ Oranges are imported into Britain. 

□ How often are these rooms cleaned? 

□ I am never invited to parties. 

□ This house was built 100 years ago. 

☐ These houses were built 100 years ago. 

□ When was the telephone invented? 

□ We weren't invited to the party last week. 

□ 'Was anybody injured in the accident?' 'Yes, two people were taken to hospital.' 

## was/were born

□ I was born in Berlin in 1989. (而不用 I am born)

□ 'Where were you born?' 'In Cairo.' 

## 被动语态 + by

☐ The telephone was invented by Alexander Bell in 1876. (= Alexander Bell invented it) 

□ I was bitten by a dog a few days ago. 

☐ Do you like these paintings? They were painted by a friend of mine. 

is being done / has been done → Unit 22 不规则动词 → Unit 24，附录 2-3 by → Unit 111

主动语态与被动语态比较→附录 1

## is being done has been done (被动语态 2)

## is/are being ... (现在进行时的被动语态)

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/8ab8fe1caeed6e22.jpg)


Somebody is painting the door. (主动)

The door is being painted. （被动）

☐ My car is at the garage. It is being repaired. (= somebody is repairing it) 

☐ Some new houses are being built opposite the park. (= somebody is building them) 

请比较现在进行时与一般现在时：

☐ The office is being cleaned at the moment. (现在进行时)

The office is cleaned every day. (一般现在时)

☐ In Britain football matches are often played at the weekend, but no matches are being played next weekend. 

关于现在进行时与一般现在时比较，参见 Unit 8 和 Unit 25。

## has/have been ... (现在完成时的被动语态)

Somebody has painted the door. (主动)

The door has been painted. （被动）

□ My key has been stolen. (= somebody has stolen it) 

☐ My keys have been stolen. (= somebody has stolen them) 

□ I'm not going to the party. I haven't been invited. (= nobody has invited me) 

□ Has this shirt been washed? (= has somebody washed it?) 

请比较现在完成时与一般过去时：

□ The room isn't dirty any more. It has been cleaned. (现在完成时)
The room was cleaned yesterday. (一般过去时)

□ I can't find my keys. I think they've been stolen. (现在完成时) My keys were stolen last week. (一般过去时)

关于现在完成时与一般过去时比较，参见 Unit 20。

## 22.1 正在发生什么事情？

1 The car is being repaired. 3 The windows  
2 A bridge 4 The grass 

## 22.2 根据下列图片，用现在进行时（is/are being ...) 或现在完成时（has/have been ...），说说正在发生或已经发生的事情。

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/0e7d55fefa689bce.jpg)


1 (the office / clean) The office is being cleaned. 

2 (the shirts / iron) The shirts have been ironed. 

3 (the window / break) The window 

4 (the roof / repair) The roof. 

5 (the car / damage) 

6 (the houses / knock / down) 

7 (the trees / cut / down) 

8 (they / invite / to a party) 

## 22.3 用括号中的词语完成句子。(参见 Unit 21。)

1 I can't use my office at the moment. It is being painted (paint). 

2 We didn't go to the party. We weren't invited (not/invite). 

3 The washing machine was broken, but it's OK now. It ____ (repair). 

4 The washing machine ____ (repair) yesterday afternoon. 

5 A factory is a place where things ____ (make). 

6 How old are these houses? When ____ (they/build)? 

7 A: ____ (the computer / use) at the moment?
B: Yes, Steve is using it. 

8 I've never seen these flowers before. What ____ (they/call)? 

9 My sunglasses ____ (steal) at the beach yesterday. 

10 The bridge is closed at the moment. It ____ (damage) last week and it ____ (not/repair) yet. 

## Unit 23

## 现在时与过去时中的 be/have/do

be (= am/is/are/was/were) + -ing (cleaning/working 等)

am/is/are + -ing
(现在进行时)
参见Units 3-4, 25

was/were + -ing
(过去进行时)
参见Unit 13

- Please be quiet. I'm working.
- It isn't raining at the moment.
- What are you doing this evening? 

□ I was working when she arrived.
□ It wasn't raining, so we didn't need an umbrella.
□ What were you doing at 3 o'clock? 

## be + 过去分词 (cleaned/made/eaten 等)

am/is/are + 过去分词
(一般现在时的被动语态)
参见Unit 21

was/were + 过去分词
(一般过去时的被动语态)
参见Unit 21

□ I'm never invited to parties.
□ Butter is made from milk.
□ These offices aren't cleaned every day. 

- The office was cleaned yesterday.
- These houses were built 100 years ago.
- How was the window broken?
- Where were you born? 

## have/has + 过去分词 (cleaned/lost/eaten/been 等)

have/has + 过去分词
(现在完成时)
参见Units 15-18

□ I've cleaned my room.
□ Tom has lost his passport.
□ Kate hasn't been to Canada.
□ Where have Paul and Nicole gone? 

## do/does/did + 动词原形 (clean/like/eat/go 等)

do/does + 动词原形
(一般现在时的否定式与疑问式)
参见Units 6-7

(一般过去时的否定式与疑问式)
参见Unit 12

□ I like coffee, but I don't like tea.
□ Chris doesn't go out very often.
□ What do you usually do at weekends?
□ Does Silvia live alone? 

□ I didn't watch TV yesterday.
□ It didn't rain last week.
□ What time did Paul and Nicole go out? 

## 23.1 填入 is/are 或 do/does。

1 ____ do ____ you work in the evenings? 6 ____ the sun shining? 

2 Where are they going? 7 What time the shops close? 

3 Why ____ you looking at me? 8 ____ Maria working today? 

4 ____ Bill live near you? 9 What ____ this word mean? 

5 ____ you like cooking? 10 ____ you feeling all right? 

## 23.2 填入 am not / isn't / aren't 或 don't/doesn't。

1 Tom doesn't work at weekends. 

2 I'm very tired. I ____ want to go out this evening. 

3 I'm very tired. I ____ going out this evening. 

4 Gary ____ working this week. He's on holiday. 

5 My parents are usually at home. They ____ go out very often. 

6 Nicole has travelled a lot, but she ____ speak any foreign languages. 

7 You can turn off the television. I ____ watching it. 

8 Liz has invited us to her party next week, but we ____ going. 

## 23.3 填入 was/were/did/have/has。

1 Where were your shoes made? 6 What time she go? 

2 ____ you go out last night? 7 When ____ these houses built? 

3 What you doing at 10.30? 8 Steve arrived yet? 

4 Where ____ your mother born? 9 Why ____ you go home early? 

5 ____ Barbara gone home? 10 How long ____ they been married? 

## 23.4 填入 is/are/was/were/have/has。

1 Joe has lost his passport. 

2 This bridge ____ built ten years ago. 

3 you finished your work yet? 

4 This town is always clean. The streets ____ cleaned every day. 

5 Where you born? 

6 I ____ just made some coffee. Would you like some? 

7 Glass ____ made from sand. 

8 This is a very old photograph. It ____ taken a long time ago. 

9 David ____ bought a new car. 

## 23.5 用方框中动词的适当形式完成句子。

<table><tr><td>damage</td><td>rain</td><td>enjoy</td><td>go</td><td>pronounce</td><td>eat</td></tr><tr><td>listen</td><td>use</td><td>open</td><td>go</td><td>understand</td><td></td></tr></table>

1 I'm going to take an umbrella with me. It's ____ raining ____. 

2 Why are you so tired? Did you go to bed late last night? 

3 Where are the chocolates? Have you ____ them all? 

4 How is your new job? Are you ____ it? 

5 My car was badly ____ in the accident, but I was OK. 

6 Chris has got a car, but she doesn't ____ it very often. 

7 Mary isn't at home. She has ____ away for a few days. 

8 I don't ____ the problem. Can you explain it again? 

9 Martin is in his room. He's ____ to music. 

10 I don't know how to say this word. How is it ____? 

11 How do you ____ this window? Can you show me? 

## 规则动词与不规则动词

## 规则动词

规则动词的过去式与过去分词以 -ed 结尾：

clean → cleaned live → lived paint → painted study → studied 

过去式（参见 Unit 11）：

□ I cleaned my room yesterday. 

□ Charlie studied engineering at university. 

## 过去分词：

现在完成时为 have/has + 过去分词（参见 Units 15-18）:

□ I have cleaned my room. 

□ Tina has lived in London for ten years. 

被动语态为 be (is/are/were/has been 等) + 过去分词 (参见 Units 21-22):

☐ These rooms are cleaned every day. 

□ My car has been repaired. 

## 不规则动词

不规则动词的过去式与过去分词不是以 -ed 结尾：

<table><tr><td>make</td><td>break</td><td>cut</td></tr><tr><td>made</td><td>broke</td><td>cut</td></tr><tr><td>made</td><td>broken</td><td>cut</td></tr></table>

有些动词的过去式与过去分词相同，例如：

<table><tr><td>make</td><td>find</td><td>buy</td><td>cut</td></tr><tr><td>made</td><td>found</td><td>bought</td><td>cut</td></tr></table>

□ I made a cake yesterday. (过去式)

☐ I have made some coffee. (过去分词：现在完成时)

□ Butter is made from milk. (过去分词：一般现在时的被动语态)

有些动词的过去式与过去分词不同，例如：

<table><tr><td>break</td><td>know</td><td>begin</td><td>go</td></tr><tr><td>broke</td><td>knew</td><td>began</td><td>went</td></tr><tr><td>broken</td><td>known</td><td>begun</td><td>gone</td></tr></table>

□ Somebody broke this window last night. (过去式)

□ Somebody has broken this window. (过去分词：现在完成时)

☐ This window was broken last night. (过去分词：一般过去时的被动语态)

## What are you doing tomorrow?

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/7d5753d512fc9efa.jpg)


They are playing tennis (now). 

today is Sunday 

I'm playing tennis tomorrow. 

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/8315fddaf98fd92f.jpg)



He is playing tennis tomorrow.


am/is/are + -ing（现在进行时）可用来表示“现在正在发生某事”：

□ 'Where are Sue and Amanda?' 'They're playing tennis in the park.' 

□ Please be quiet. I'm working. 

am/is/are + -ing 也可用来表示将来 (tomorrow / next week 等):

□ Andrew is playing tennis tomorrow. 

□ I'm not working next week. 

I am doing something tomorrow 表示 “我已安排好明天要做某事 / 我计划明天做某事”

- Sophie is going to the dentist on Friday. (= she has an appointment with the dentist)
- We're having a party next weekend.
- Are you meeting your friends tonight?
- What are you doing tomorrow evening?
- I'm not going out tonight. I'm staying at home. 

也可说 I'm going to do something (参见 Unit 26)。

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/53845679abecb364.jpg)


要注意，不用一般现在时 (I stay / do you go 等) 表示计划与安排：

□ I'm staying at home this evening. (而不用 I stay)

□ Are you going out tonight? (而不用 Do you go)

□ Lisa isn't coming to the party next week. (而不用 Lisa doesn't come)

但用一般现在时表示时间表、节目单、火车与公共汽车时刻表等：

□ The train arrives at 7.30. 

□ What time does the film finish? 

请比较：

现在进行时——通常指人

一般现在时——指时间表、节目单等

□ I'm going to a concert tomorrow. 

□ What time are you leaving? 

□ The concert starts at 7.30. 

□ What time does your train leave?

## 25.4 用动词的现在进行时（he is leaving 等）或一般现在时（the train leaves 等）形式填空。

1 'Are you going (you/go) out tonight?' 'No, I'm too tired.'  
2 We're going (we/go) to a concert tonight. It starts (it/start) at 7.30.  
3 Do you know about Sally? (she/get) married next month!  
4 A: My parents (go) on holiday next week.  
B: Oh, that's nice. Where (they/go)? 

5 Silvia is doing an English course at the moment. The course ____ (finish) on Friday.
6 There's a party tomorrow night, but ____ (I/not/go). 

7 (I/go) out with some friends tonight. Why don't you come too? (we/meet) outside the Royal Hotel at 8 o'clock. 

8 A: How ____ (you/get) home after the party tomorrow? By taxi?
B: No, I can go by bus. The last bus ____ (leave) at midnight.

B: Yes, what time ____ (the film / begin)?

B: ____ (I/work). 

<table><tr><td>I amhe/she/it iswe/you/they are</td><td colspan="2">(not) going to</td><td>do ...drink ...watch ...</td></tr><tr><td>am Iis he/she/itare we/you/they</td><td>going to</td><td>buy ... ?eat ... ?wear ... ?</td><td></td></tr></table>

## I'm going to ...

## I'm going to do something

I'm going to watch TV this evening. 

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/6351c745cb3c6089.jpg)


She is going to watch TV this evening. 

am/is/are going to ... 表示将来:

I am going to do something 表示 “我已决定做某事 / 我的意图是做某事”：

I decided to do it → I'm going to do it 

过去

现在

将来

□ I'm going to buy some books tomorrow. 

□ Sarah is going to sell her car. 

□ I'm not going to have breakfast this morning. I'm not hungry. 

□ What are you going to wear to the wedding next week? 

□ 'Your hands are dirty.' 'Yes, I know. I'm going to wash them.' 

□ Are you going to invite Martin to your party? 

也用现在进行时 (I am doing) 表示将来，常指安排（参见 Unit 25）：

□ I am playing tennis with Julia tomorrow. 

## something is going to happen

something is going to happen 表示 “从现在来看某事肯定要发生”：

□ Look at the sky! It's going to rain.
(现在有乌云 → 肯定要下雨)

□ Oh dear! It's 9 o'clock and I'm not ready. I'm going to be late. 

(现在9点钟，还没准备好→肯定要迟到)

## 6.4 你今天或明天打算做什么？写三句话。

1 I'm .....
2 .....
3 .... 

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/85866f7f6a5bb124.jpg)


SARAH 

Sarah goes to work every day. She is always there from 8.30 until 4.30. 

依据此意可知：

It is 11 o'clock now. Sarah is at work. 

At 11 o'clock yesterday, she was at work. 

At 11 o'clock tomorrow, she will be at work. 

will + 动词原形 (will be / will win / will come 等):

<table><tr><td>I/we/you/they he/she/it</td><td>will (’ll) will not (won’t)</td><td>be win eat come 等</td><td>will</td><td>I/we/you/they he/she/it</td><td>be? win? eat? come? 等</td></tr></table>

'll = will: I'll (= I will) / you'll / she'll 等
won't = will not: I won't (= I will not) / you won't / she won't 等

B will 表示将来 (tomorrow / next week 等):

- Sue travels a lot. Today she is in Madrid. Tomorrow she'll be in Rome. Next week she'll be in Tokyo.
- You can call me this evening. I'll be at home.
- Leave the old bread in the garden. The birds will eat it.
- We'll probably go out this evening.
- Will you be at home this evening?
- I won't be here tomorrow. (= I will not be here)
- Don't drink coffee before you go to bed. You won't sleep. 

常用 I think ... will ... 结构：
□ I think Kelly will pass the exam.
□ I don't think it will rain this afternoon.
□ Do you think the exam will be difficult?

will 不用来表示已经安排好或决定做的事情（参见 Units 25–26）：
□ We're going to the cinema on Saturday. Do you want to come with us? (而不用 We will go)
□ I'm not working tomorrow. (而不用 I won't work)
□ Are you going to do the exam? (而不用 Will you do)

## shall

可以用 I shall (= I will) 与 we shall (= we will):
□ I shall be late tomorrow. 或 I will (I'll) be late tomorrow.
□ I think we shall win. 或 I think we will (we'll) win.

在构成将来时的时候，不可将 shall 与 you/they/he/she/it 等非第一人称连用：
□ Tom will be late. (而不用 Tom shall be)

27.1 海伦正在欧洲旅行。用 she was, she's 或 she'll be 完成下列句子。

1 Yesterday she was in Paris.  
2 Tomorrow in Amsterdam.  
3 Last week in Barcelona.  
4 Next week in London.  
5 At the moment in Brussels.  
6 Three days ago in Munich.  
7 At the end of her trip very tired.

27.3 填入 will ('ll) 或 won't。

1 Don't drink coffee before you go to bed. You ____ sleep.
2 'Are you ready yet?' 'Not yet. I ____ be ready in five minutes.'
3 I'm going away for a few days. I'm leaving tonight, so I ____ be at home tomorrow.
4 It ____ rain, so you don't need to take an umbrella.
5 A: I don't feel very well this evening.
    B: Well, go to bed early and you ____ feel better in the morning.
6 It's Bill's birthday next Monday. He ____ be 25.
7 I'm sorry I was late this morning. It ____ happen again.

27.4 用 I think ... 或 I don't think ... 句式造句。
1 (Kelly will pass the exam) I think Kelly will pass the exam.
2 (Kelly won't pass the exam) I don't think Kelly will pass the exam.
3 (we'll win the game) I
4 (I won't be here tomorrow)
5 (Sue will like her present)
6 (they won't get married)
7 (you won't enjoy the film)

## 27.5 从画线部分中选出正确的表达方式。(参见 Unit 25。)

1 We'll go / We're going to the theatre tonight. We've got tickets. (We're going is right)
2 'What will you do / are you doing tomorrow evening?' 'Nothing. I'm free.'
3 They'll go / They're going away tomorrow morning. Their train is at 8.40.
4 I'm sure your aunt will lend / is lending us some money. She's very rich.
5 'Why are you putting on your coat?' 'I'll go / I'm going out.'
6 Do you think Claire will phone / is phoning us tonight?
7 Steve can't meet us on Saturday. He'll work / He's working.
8 Will you / Shall you be at home tomorrow evening?
9 A: What are your plans for the weekend?
B: Some friends will come / are coming to stay with us. 

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/00a5cc3a8f449b27.jpg)


I'll (I will) ... 可表示提议或决定做某事：
□ 'My bag is very heavy.' 'I'll carry it for you.'
□ 'I'll phone you tomorrow, OK?' 'OK, bye.'

I think I'll ... / I don't think I'll ... 可表示决定做某事：
□ I'm tired. I think I'll go to bed early tonight.
□ It's a nice day. I think I'll sit outside.
□ It's raining. I don't think I'll go out.

有些句子中不用一般现在时 (I go / I phone 等)，例如：
□ I'll phone you tomorrow, OK? (而不用 I phone you)
□ I think I'll go to bed early. (而不用 I go to bed)

I'll ... 不用来表示事先决定好的事情 (参见 Units 25-26):  
□ I'm working tomorrow. (而不用 I'll work)  
□ There's a good film on TV tonight. I'm going to watch it. (而不用 I'll watch)  
□ What are you doing at the weekend? (而不用 What will you do)

## Shall I ... ? Shall we ... ?

No, it's OK. I'll answer it. 

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/cf3a930ac0be264f.jpg)


Shall I / Shall we ... ? 表示 “你认为……好吗？/ 你认为……是个好办法吗？”

□ It's very warm in this room. Shall I open the window? 

□ 'Shall I phone you this evening?' 'Yes, please.' 

□ I'm going to a party tonight. What shall I wear? 

□ It's a nice day. Shall we go for a walk? 

□ Where shall we go for our holidays this year? 

□ 'Let's go out this evening.' 'OK, what time shall we meet?' 

28.1 用 I'll (I will) + 下列动词完成句子。

carry do eat send show sit stay 

My bag is very heavy. Enjoy your holiday. I don't want this banana. Do you want a chair? Did you phone Jenny? Are you coming with me? How do you use this camera? 

I'll carry it for you. Thank you. you a postcard. Well, I'm hungry. it. No, it's OK. on the floor. Oh no, I forgot. it now. No, I don't think so. here. Give it to me and you. 

## 28.2 用 I think I'll ... 或 I don't think I'll ... 句式及下列动词完成句子。

## buy buy go have play

## 28.3 从画线部分中选出正确的表达方式。

1 I phone / I'll phone you tomorrow, OK? (I'll phone is right)
2 I haven't done the shopping yet. I do / I'll do it later.
3 I like sport. I watch / I'll watch a lot of sport on TV.
4 I need some exercise. I think I go / I'll go for a walk.

7 A: Are you doing / Will you do anything this evening?
B: Yes, I'm going / I'll go out with some friends.
8 I can't go out with you tomorrow night. I work / I'm working / I'll work.

He might go to New York. It might rain. (= it is possible that he will go to New York) (= it is possible that it will rain) 

## might + 动词原形 (might go / might be / might rain 等):

<table><tr><td>I/we/you/they he/she/it</td><td>might (not)</td><td>be go play come 等</td></tr></table>

## I might 表示 “我可能”

□ I might go to the cinema this evening, but I'm not sure. (= it is possible that I will go) 

□ A: When is Rebecca going to phone you? 

B: I don't know. She might phone this afternoon. 

□ Take an umbrella with you. It might rain. 

□ Buy a lottery ticket. You might be lucky. (= perhaps you will be lucky) 

□ 'Are you going out tonight?' 'I might.' (= I might go out) 

## 请比较下列句子：

□ I'm playing tennis tomorrow. (肯定)

I might play tennis tomorrow. (可能)

□ Rebecca is going to phone later. (肯定)
Rebecca might phone later. (可能)

## I might not 为否定式，表示 “我可能不”：

☐ I might not go to work tomorrow. (= it is possible that I will not go) 

□ Sue might not come to the party. (= it is possible that she will not come) 

## may

may 和 might 用法相同。I may = I might:

☐ I may go to the cinema this evening. (= I might go) 

□ Sue may not come to the party. (= Sue might not come) 

May I ... ? 表示 “我……好吗？ / 我能……吗？”：

□ May I ask a question? (= is it OK to ask / can I ask?) 

□ 'May I sit here?' 'Yes, of course.' 

## 29.1 用 might 造句。

1 (it's possible that I'll go to the cinema)  
2 (it's possible that I'll see you tomorrow)  
3 (it's possible that Sarah will forget to phone)  
4 (it's possible that it will snow today)  
5 (it's possible that I'll be late tonight) 

I might go to the cinema. 

用 might not 造句。
6 (it's possible that Mark will not be here next week)
7 (it's possible that I won't have time to go out)

## 29.4 写出你明天可能做的三件事情。

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/dba98320ea6db8d0.jpg)


He can play the piano. 

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/3dc01ef4a30cb88f.jpg)


can + 动词原形 (can do / can play / can come 等):

<table><tr><td>I/we/you/they he/she/it</td><td>can can&#x27;t (cannot)</td><td>do play see come 等</td><td>can</td><td>I/we/you/they he/she/it</td><td>do? play? see? come? 等</td></tr></table>

I can (do something) 表示 “知道如何（做某事）或有可能（做某事）”：

□ I can play the piano. My brother can play the piano too. 

□ Sarah can speak Italian, but she can't speak Spanish. 

□ 'Can you swim?' 'Yes, but I'm not a very good swimmer.' 

□ 'Can you change twenty pounds?' 'I'm sorry, I can't.' 

□ I'm having a party next week, but Paul and Rachel can't come. 

表示过去 (yesterday / last week 等) 时，用 could/couldn't:

□ When I was young, I could run very fast. 

Before Maria came to Britain, she couldn't understand much English. Now she can understand everything. 

□ I was tired last night, but I couldn't sleep. 

□ I had a party last week, but Paul and Rachel couldn't come. 

Can you ... ? Could you ... ? Can I ... ? Could I ... ? 

Can you ...? 或 Could you ...? 用于请求对方做某事：

□ Can you open the door, please? 或 Could you open the door, please?

□ Can you wait a moment, please? 或 Could you wait ... ?

Can I have ...? 或 Could I have ...? 用于向对方要求某物：

☐ (in a shop) Can I have these postcards, please? 或 Could I have ...?

Can I ... ? 或 Could I ... ? 用于向对方征询意见：

□ Tom, can I borrow your umbrella? 或 Tom, could I borrow your umbrella?

□ (on the phone) Hello, can I speak to Gary, please? 或 ... could I speak ...?

## 30.4 在下列情形中你会说些什么？要求用上 can 或 could 以及括号中的词语。

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/3e643b8ac9bcdcbf.jpg)


![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/3f6c0e7f12ba9ec2.jpg)


It's a fantastic film. You must see it. 

must + 动词原形 (must do / must work 等):

<table><tr><td>I/we/you/they he/she/it</td><td>must</td><td>dogoseeat等</td></tr></table>

I must (do something) 表示 “我有必要（做某事）”：

□ I'm very hungry. I must eat something. 

□ It's a fantastic film. You must see it. 

☐ The windows are very dirty. We must clean them. 

表示过去 (yesterday / last week 等) 时，用 had to ... (而不用 must):

□ I was very hungry. I had to eat something. (而不用 I must eat)

□ We had to walk home last night. There were no buses. (而不用 We must walk)

## mustn't (= must not)

I mustn't (do something) 表示 “我一定不要，千万不要（做某事）”：

□ I must hurry. I mustn't be late. 

□ I mustn't forget to phone Jane. 

(= I must remember to phone her) 

□ Be happy! You mustn't be sad. (= don't be sad) 

□ You mustn't touch the pictures. (= don't touch the pictures) 

You mustn't touch the pictures. 

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/4ab0ea179d501c76.jpg)


## don't need to

I don't need (to do something) 表示 “我没必要（做某事）或不必（做某事）”：

□ I don't need to go yet. I can stay a little longer. 

□ You don't need to shout. I can hear you OK. 

也可以说 don't have to ...:

□ I don't have to go yet. I can stay a little longer. 

请比较 don't need to 与 mustn't:

□ You don't need to go. You can stay here if you want. 

□ You mustn't go. You must stay here.

You shouldn't watch TV so much. 

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/5755e09720fc273a.jpg)


## should + 动词原形

(should do / should watch 等):

<table><tr><td>I/we/you/they he/she/it</td><td>should shouldn&#x27;t</td><td>do stop go watch 等</td></tr></table>

you should do something 表示 “做某事是好的或是对的”：

□ Tom doesn't study enough. He should study harder. 

□ It's a good film. You should go and see it. 

□ When you play tennis, you should always watch the ball. 

you shouldn't do something 表示 “做某事是不好的”。

shouldn't = should not: 

□ Tom shouldn't go to bed so late. 

□ You watch TV all the time. You shouldn't watch TV so much. 

## I think 常与 should 连用：

肯定句用 I think ... should ...:

☐ I think Lisa should buy some new clothes. 

(= I think it is a good idea.) 

□ It's late. I think I should go home now. 

□ A: Shall I buy this coat? 

B: Yes, I think you should. 

否定句用 I don't think ... should ...:

□ I don't think you should work so hard. 

(= I don't think it is a good idea.) 

□ I don't think we should go yet. It's too early. 

疑问句用 Do you think ... should ... ?:

□ Do you think I should buy this hat? 

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/460bf1485210fcac.jpg)


□ What time do you think we should go home? 

must 比 should 语气更强烈：

□ It's a good film. You should go and see it. 

□ It's a fantastic film. You must go and see it. 

也可用 ought to 代替 should:

□ It's a good film. You ought to go and see it. (= you should go) 

☐ I think Lisa ought to buy some new clothes. (= Lisa should buy) 

shall → Units 27-28 must → Unit 31

I have to (do something) 表示 “我必须或有义务（做某事）”：

<table><tr><td>I/we/you/they have</td><td rowspan="2">to do to work to go to wear 等</td></tr><tr><td>he/she/it has</td></tr></table>

□ I'll be late for work tomorrow. I have to go to the dentist. 

□ Jane starts work at 7 o'clock, so she has to get up at 6. 

☐ You have to pass a test before you can get a driving licence. 

表示过去 (yesterday / last week 等) 时，用 had to ...:

□ I was late for work yesterday. I had to go to the dentist. 

□ We had to walk home last night. There were no buses. 

## 在疑问句与否定句中用 do/does（现在时）与 did（过去时）：

现在时

<table><tr><td>do I/we/you/they</td><td rowspan="2">have to ... ?</td></tr><tr><td>does he/she/it</td></tr></table>

<table><tr><td>I/we/you/they don&#x27;t</td><td rowspan="2">have to ...</td></tr><tr><td>he/she/it doesn&#x27;t</td></tr></table>

过去时

<table><tr><td>did</td><td>I/we/you/they he/she/it</td><td>have to ... ?</td></tr></table>

<table><tr><td>I/we/you/they he/she/it</td><td>didn&#x27;t have to ...</td></tr></table>

□ What time do you have to go to the dentist tomorrow? 

□ Does Jane have to work on Sundays? 

□ Why did they have to leave the party early? 

I don't have to (do something) 表示 “我没有必要（做某事）”：

□ I'm not working tomorrow, so I don't have to get up early. 

□ Ian doesn't have to work very hard. He's got an easy job. 

□ We didn't have to wait very long for the bus – it came in a few minutes. 

## must 与 have to 比较

must 或 have to 可用来表示认为有必要做某事或提出个人看法：

□ It's a fantastic film. You must see it. 或 You have to see it.

不是表达个人看法时用 have to (而不用 must)。请比较：

□ Jane won't be at work this afternoon. She has to go to the doctor. 

(不是表达个人看法，而是陈述事实)

□ Jane isn't well. She doesn't want to go to the doctor, but I told her she must go. (是表达个人看法)

## Would you like ...? 表示“你想要……吗”。

## Would you like ...? 用来表示提供某物：

□ A: Would you like some coffee? 

B: No, thank you. 

□ A: Would you like a chocolate? 

B: Yes, please. 

□ A: What would you like, tea or coffee?
B: Tea, please. 

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/a984a79daee59c23.jpg)


## Would you like to ...? 可用来表示邀请某人:

□ Would you like to go for a walk? 

□ A: Would you like to have dinner with us on Sunday? 

B: Yes, I'd love to. (= I would love to have dinner with you) 

□ What would you like to do this evening? 

I'd like ... 是 I want ... 的礼貌说法。I'd like = I would like:

□ I'm thirsty. I'd like a drink. 

☐ (in a tourist office) I'd like some information about hotels, please. 

□ I'm feeling tired. I'd like to stay at home this evening. 

## Would you like ...? 与 Do you like ...? 比较

Would you like ... ? / I'd like ... 

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/990d6a84e4a81e9f.jpg)


## Would you like some tea? 表示 “你想喝茶吗”。

□ A: Would you like to go to the cinema tonight? 

(= do you want to go tonight?) 

Do you like ... ? / I like ... 

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/0761a1a2c1b0f0a1.jpg)


B: Yes, I'd love to. 

Do you like tea? 表示 “你喜欢喝茶吗”。

□ I'd like an orange, please. (= can I have an orange?) 

□ A: Do you like going to the cinema?
(询问喜好)

□ What would you like to do next weekend? 

B: Yes, I go to the cinema a lot. 

□ I like oranges. (表示喜好)

□ What do you like to do at weekends? 

34.1 图中的人物在说些什么？要求使用 Would you like ... ?句式。

34.2 在下列情况下你会对休说什么？要求用上 Would you like to ... ?句式。

1 You want to go to the cinema tonight. Perhaps Sue will go with you. (go) You say: Would you like to go to the cinema tonight? 

2 You want to play tennis tomorrow. Perhaps Sue will play too. (play) You say: ____ 

3 You have an extra ticket for a concert next week. Perhaps Sue will come. (come) You say: 

4 It's raining and Sue is going out. She hasn't got an umbrella, but you have one. (borrow) You say: ____ 

## 34.3 从画线部分中选出正确的表达方式。

1 'Do you like / Would you like a chocolate?' 'Yes, please.' (Would you like is right) 

2 'Do you like / Would you like bananas?' 'Yes, I love them.' 

3 'Do you like / Would you like an ice-cream?' 'No, thank you.' 

4 'What do you like / would you like to drink?' 'A glass of water, please.' 

5 'Do you like / Would you like to go out for a walk?' 'Not now. Perhaps later.' 

6 I like / I'd like tomatoes, but I don't eat them very often. 

7 What time do you like / would you like to have dinner this evening? 

8 'Do you like / Would you like something to eat?' 'No, thanks. I'm not hungry.' 

9 'Do you like / Would you like your new job?' 'Yes, I'm enjoying it.' 

10 I'm tired. I like / I'd like to go to sleep now. 

11 'I like / I'd like a sandwich, please.' 'Sure. What kind of sandwich?' 

12 'What kind of music do you like / would you like?' 'All kinds.' 

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/d682be740f758a09.jpg)


come/look/go/wait/do/be 等可用来命令或吩咐某人做某事：

□ 'Come here and look at this!' 'What is it?' 

□ I don't want to talk to you. Go away! 

□ I'm not ready yet. Please wait for me. 

□ Please be quiet. I'm working. 

也可以说：

□ Bye! Have a good holiday! / Have a nice time! / Have a good flight! / Have fun! (= I hope you have a good holiday 等)
□ 'Have a chocolate.' 'Oh, thanks.' (= would you like a chocolate?)

don't ... 可用来劝告某人不要做某事：
□ Be careful! Don't fall.
□ Please don't go. Stay here with me.
□ Be here on time. Don't be late.

let's ... 可用来提议一起做某事。let's = let us:

It's a nice day. Let's go out. (= you and I can go out)  
Come on! Let's dance. (= you and I can dance)  
Are you ready? Let's go.  
Let's have fish for dinner tonight.  
A: Shall we go out tonight?  
B: No, I'm tired. Let's stay at home. 

否定形式为 let's not ...:

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/54a59c9567926f0d.jpg)


□ It's cold. Let's not go out. Let's stay at home. 

Are you ready? Let's go. 

□ Let's not have fish for dinner tonight. Let's have chicken. 

也可以说 don't let's ...:

□ It's cold. Don't let's go out. Let's stay at home.

Dave used to work in a factory. Now he works in a supermarket. 

Dave used to work in a factory 表示戴夫以前在工厂工作，但现在不在那里工作了：

<table><tr><td>he used to work</td><td>he works</td></tr><tr><td>过去</td><td>现在</td></tr></table>

可以说 I used to work ... / she used to have ... / they used to be ... 等：

<table><tr><td>I/you/we/they he/she/it</td><td>used to</td><td>be work have play 等</td></tr></table>

□ When I was a child, I used to like chocolate. 

□ I used to read a lot of books, but I don't read much these days. 

□ Liz has got short hair now, but it used to be very long. 

□ They used to live in the same street as us, so we used to see them a lot. But we don't see them very often these days. 

□ Helen used to have a piano, but she sold it a few years ago. 

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/22db8917f275ce6d.jpg)


## 否定式为 I didn't use to ...:

□ When I was a child, I didn't use to like tomatoes. 

疑问式为 did you use to ...?

□ Where did you use to live before you came here? 

used to ... 仅用于表示过去。不能用 I use to ... 表示现在：

☐ I used to play tennis. These days I play golf. (而不用 I use to play golf)

□ We usually get up early. (而不用 We use to get up early)

## 单数

there is ... (there's) 

is there ... ? 

there is not ... (there isn't 

或 there's not)

复数

there are 

are there ... ? 

there are not ... (there aren't) 

□ There's a big tree in the garden. 

□ There's nothing on TV tonight. 

□ A: Have you got any money? 

B: Yes, there's some in my bag. 

□ A: Excuse me, is there a hotel near here? 

B: Yes, there is. / No, there isn't. 

□ We can't go skiing. There isn't any snow. 

☐ There are some big trees in the garden. 

☐ There are a lot of accidents on this road. 

□ A: Are there any restaurants near here?
B: Yes, there are. / No, there aren't. 

□ This restaurant is very quiet. There aren't many people here. 

□ How many players are there in a football team? 

☐ There are 11 players in a football team. 

## there is 与 it is 比较

## there is

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/7374b6e2b0c2bcbc.jpg)


There's a book on the table. 

(而不用 It's a book on the table.)

it is 

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/0ab02fdbb16c8568.jpg)


I like this book. It's interesting. (It = this book) 

## 请比较：

□ 'What's that noise?' 'It's a train.' (It = that noise) 

There's a train at 10.30. It's a fast train. (It = the 10.30 train) 

□ There's a lot of salt in this soup. 

I don't like this soup. It's too salty. (It = this soup)

## Unit 38

## there was/were there has/have been there will be

## there was / there were (过去时)

## STATION

There is a train every hour. 

The time now is 11.15. 

There was a train at 11 o'clock. 

## 请比较：

there is/are (一般现在时)

☐ There is a good film on TV tonight. 

□ We are staying at a very big hotel.
There are 550 rooms. 

□ Are there any phone messages for me this morning? 

□ I'm hungry, but there isn't anything to eat. 

## there was/were (一般过去时)

☐ There was a good film on TV last night. 

□ We stayed at a very big hotel.
There were 550 rooms. 

□ Were there any phone messages for me yesterday? 

□ I was hungry when I got home, but there wasn't anything to eat. 

## there has been / there have been (现在完成时)

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/535d33cd333104a7.jpg)


□ Look! There's been an accident. 

(there's been = there has been) 

☐ This road is very dangerous. There have been many accidents. 

请与 there was (一般过去时) 比较:

□ There was an accident last night. 

(而不用 There has been an accident last night.)

## there will be (一般将来时)

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/8161e57263b7e7ae.jpg)


关于一般过去时与现在完成时比较，参见 Unit 20。

☐ Do you think there will be a lot of people at the party on Saturday? 

☐ The manager of the company is leaving, so there will be a new manager soon. 

□ I'm going away tomorrow. I'll do my packing today because there won't be time tomorrow. 

(there won't be = there will not be)

## Unit 39

## It ...

## it 表示时间、日期、距离和天气：

## 时间

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/8e26cf29cb065356.jpg)


□ What time is it? 

□ It's half past ten. 

□ It's late. 

□ It's time to go home. 

## 日期

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/3edd359198a5013f.jpg)


□ What day is it? 

□ It's Thursday. 

□ It's 16 March. 

□ It was my birthday yesterday. 

## 距离

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/053f23827f5b2c22.jpg)


天气

□ It's three kilometres from our house to the city centre. 

□ How far is it from New York to Los Angeles? 

□ It's a long way from here to the station. 

□ We can walk home. It isn't far. 

far 用于疑问句 (is it far?) 与否定句 (it isn't far) 中。
a long way 用于肯定句 (it's a long way) 中。

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/fd10820eeaf8c878.jpg)


□ It's raining. It isn't raining. Is it snowing? 

□ It rains a lot here. It didn't rain yesterday. Does it snow very often? 

It's warm/hot/cold/fine/cloudy/windy/sunny/foggy/dark etc. 

□ It's a nice day today. 

## 请比较 it 与 there:

☐ It rains a lot in winter. 

There is a lot of rain in winter. 

□ It was very windy. 

There was a strong wind yesterday. 

## It's nice to ... 句式:

<table><tr><td>It&#x27;s</td><td>easy / difficult / impossible / dangerous / safe expensive / interesting / nice / wonderful / terrible 等</td><td>to ...</td></tr></table>

□ It's nice to see you again. 

□ It's impossible to understand her. 

□ It wasn't easy to find your house. 

注意 it 不能省略：
□ It's raining again. (而不用 Is raining again)
□ Is it true that you're going away? (而不用 Is true that ...)
