## 39.5 从方框中选择恰当的词语完成下列句子。

<table><tr><td>easydifficultimpossible</td><td>dangerousniceinteresting</td><td>to</td><td>work in this officevisit different placessee you again</td><td>get up earlygo out alonemake friends</td></tr></table>

1 If you go to bed late, it's difficult to get up early in the morning. 

2 Hello, Jane. 

4 Everybody is very nice at work. 

5 I like travelling. 

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/9e5ae5d551ccf4d1.jpg)


She isn't tired, but he is. 

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/372ac505b5e971a6.jpg)


(he is = he is tired) 

He likes tea, but she doesn't. 

(she doesn't = she doesn't like tea) 

上述例句中，不必再重复出现 tired，like tea。

## 下框中的动词可以这样用：

am/is/are 

□ I haven't got a car, but my sister has. (= my sister has got a car) 

was/were 

have/has 

□ A: Please help me. 

do/does/did 

B: I'm sorry. I can't. (= I can't help you) 

□ A: Are you tired? 

can 

B: I was, but I'm not now. (= I was tired, but I'm not tired now) 

will 

□ A: Do you think Jane will phone this evening? 

might 

B: She might. (= she might phone) 

must 

□ A: Are you going now? 

B: Yes, I'm afraid I must. (= I must go) 

不能用 'm/’s/’ve 等（缩略形式），必须用 am/is/have 等：

□ She isn't tired, but he is. (而不用 ... but he's)

但可用 isn't / haven't / won't 等（否定缩略形式）:

□ My sister has got a car, but I haven't. 

□ 'Are you and Jane working tomorrow?' 'I am, but Jane isn't.' 

## I am / I'm not 等可用于 Yes 和 No 之后：

□ 'Are you tired?' 'Yes, I am. / No, I'm not.' 

□ 'Will Alan be here tomorrow?' 'Yes, he will. / No, he won't.' 

□ 'Is there a bus to the airport?' 'Yes, there is. / No, there isn't.' 

## do/does 表示一般现在时（参见 Units 6-7）:

□ I don't like hot weather, but Sue does. (= Sue likes hot weather) 

□ Sue works hard, but I don't. (= I don't work hard) 

□ 'Do you enjoy your work?' 'Yes, I do.' 

## did 表示一般过去时（参见 Unit 12）：

□ A: Did you and Chris enjoy the film? 

B: I did, but Chris didn't. (= I enjoyed it, but Chris didn't enjoy it) 

□ 'I had a good time.' 'I did too.' (= I enjoyed it too) 

□ 'Did it rain yesterday?' 'No, it didn't.' 

40.1 完成下列句子，要求每次只用一个动词（is/have/can 等）。
1 Kate wasn't hungry, but we ____ . 4 I haven't seen the film, but Tom .....
2 I'm not married, but my brother .... . 5 Karen won't be here, but Chris .....
3 Bill can't help you, but I .... . 6 You weren't late, but I .....
40.2 用动词的否定式（isn't/haven't/can't 等）完成下列句子。
1 My sister can play the piano, but I ____ . 4 Mark has been to China, but I .....
2 Sam is working today, but I .... . 5 I'm ready to go, but Tom .....
3 I was working, but my friends .... . 6 I've got a key, but Sally .....
40.3 用 do/does/did 或 don't/doesn't/didn't 完成下列句子。
1 I don't like hot weather, but Sue ____ .
2 Sue likes hot weather, but I ____ . 
3 My mother wears glasses, but my father .....
4 You don't know Paul very well, but I .....
5 I didn't enjoy the party, but my friends .....
6 I don't watch TV much, but Peter .....
7 Kate lives in London, but her parents .....
8 You had breakfast this morning, but I .....
40.4 仿照示例，根据你自己与别人的情况完成句子。
1 I didn't ____ go out last night, but my friends did.
2 I like ____, but .....
3 I don't ____, but .....
4 I'm .....
5 I haven't .....
40.5 用动词的肯定式或否定式填空。
1 'Are you tired?' 'I ____ earlier, but I'm not now.'
2 Steve is happy today, but he ____ yesterday.
3 The post office isn't open yet, but the shops .....
4 I haven't got a telescope, but I know somebody who .....
5 I would like to help you, but I'm afraid I .....
6 I don't usually go to work by car, but I ____ yesterday.
7 A: Have you ever been to the United States?
B: No, but Sandra ____ . She went there on holiday last year.
8 'Do you and Chris watch TV a lot?' 'I ____ , but Chris doesn't.'
9 I've been invited to Sam's wedding, but Kate .....
10 'Do you think Sarah will pass her driving test?' 'Yes, I'm sure she ____.'
11 'Are you going out tonight?' 'I ____ . I don't know for sure.'
40.6 根据你自己的情况，用 Yes, I have. / No, I'm not. 等回答下列问题。
1 Are you American? No, I'm not.
2 Have you got a car?
3 Do you feel OK?
4 Is it snowing?
5 Are you hungry?
6 Do you like classical music?
7 Will you be in Paris tomorrow?
8 Have you ever broken your arm?
9 Did you buy anything yesterday?
10 Were you asleep at 3 a.m.?

## Exercises

I'm writing a book. 

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/fe501949ac0fdde0.jpg)


## have you? / is it? / can't he? 等可用来表示对某事感兴趣或感到惊奇：

□ 'You're late.' 'Oh, am I? I'm sorry.' 

□ 'I was ill last week.' 'Were you? I didn't know that.' 

□ 'It's raining again.' 'Is it? It was sunny ten minutes ago.' 

□ 'There's a letter for you.' 'Is there? Where is it?' 

□ 'Bill can't drive.' 'Can't he? I didn't know that.' 

□ 'I'm not hungry.' 'Aren't you? I am.' 

□ 'Sue isn't at work today.' 'Isn't she? Is she ill?' 

do/does 表示一般现在时，did 表示一般过去时：

□ 'I speak four languages.' 'Do you? Which ones?' 

□ 'Tim doesn't eat meat.' 'Doesn't he? Does he eat fish?' 

□ 'Nicole got married last week.' 'Did she? Really?' 

## 附加疑问句

have you? / is it? / can't she? 等

可作为附加疑问句用于句尾。

肯定句之后的附加疑问句用否定式。

否定句之后的附加疑问句用肯定式。

It's a beautiful day, isn't it? 

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/d5cc938cb1ff5899.jpg)


Yes, it's perfect. 

## 先肯定，后否定

It's a beautiful day, isn't it? 

Sally lives in London, doesn't she? 

Yes, it's perfect. 

You closed the window, didn't you? 

Yes, that's right. 

Those shoes are nice, aren't they? 

Yes, I think so. 

Tom will be here soon, won't he? 

Yes, very nice. 

Yes, probably. 

## 先否定，后肯定

That isn't your car, is it? 

No, it's my mother's. 

You haven't met my mother, have you? 

Sally doesn't go out much, does she? 

No, I haven't. 

You won't be late, will you? 

No, she doesn't. 

No, I'm never late.

## too 与 either 比较

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/7264f9833f5f6ba9.jpg)


![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/3e2c9a35f8a4c701.jpg)


![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/41c07101e6da00f0.jpg)


I'm not happy either. 

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/e127a1301d8d7324.jpg)


## too 与 either 用于句尾。

too 用于肯定形式的动词之后：

□ A: I'm happy. 

B: I'm happy too. 

□ A: I enjoyed the film. 

B: I enjoyed it too. 

□ Jane is a doctor. Her husband is a doctor too. 

either 用于否定形式的动词之后：

□ A: I'm not happy. 

B: I'm not happy either.
(而不用 I'm not ... too)

□ A: I can't cook. 

B: I can't either. (而不用 I can't too)

□ Bill doesn't watch TV. He doesn't read newspapers either. 

## so am I / neither do I 等

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/3e2e6e535edb8314.jpg)


<table><tr><td>so neither</td><td>am/is/are ... was/were ... do/does ... did ... have/has ... can ... will ... would ...</td></tr></table>

## so am I = I am too

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/bc3bf18ce9618a11.jpg)


so have I = I have too 等:

□ A: I'm working. 

B: So am I. (= I'm working too) 

□ A: I was late for work today. 

B: So was Sam. (= Sam was late too) 

□ A: I work in a bank.
B: So do I. 

□ A: We went to the cinema last night. 

B: Did you? So did we. 

□ A: I'd like to go to Australia. 

B: So would I. 

## neither am I = I'm not either

neither can I = I can't either 等:

□ A: I haven't got a key. 

B: Neither have I. (= I haven't either) 

□ A: Kate can't cook. 

B: Neither can Tom. (= Tom can't either) 

□ A: I won't (= will not) be here tomorrow. 

B: Neither will I. 

□ A: I never go to the cinema. 

B: Neither do I. 

也可用 nor 代替 neither:

□ A: I'm not married. 

B: Nor am I. 或 Neither am I.

注意应说：so am I (而不用 so I am), neither have I (而不用 neither I have)。

## isn't, haven't, don't 等（否定句）

## 否定句中用 not (n't):

## 肯定式 $\rightarrow$ 否定式

<table><tr><td>am</td><td>am not (&#x27;m not)</td><td>□ I&#x27;m not tired.</td></tr><tr><td>is</td><td>is not (isn&#x27;t 或 &#x27;s not)</td><td>□ It isn&#x27;t (或 It&#x27;s not) raining.</td></tr><tr><td>are</td><td>are not (aren&#x27;t 或 &#x27;re not)</td><td>□ They aren&#x27;t (或 They&#x27;re not) here.</td></tr><tr><td>was</td><td>was not (wasn&#x27;t)</td><td>□ Julian wasn&#x27;t hungry.</td></tr><tr><td>were</td><td>were not (weren&#x27;t)</td><td>□ The shops weren&#x27;t open.</td></tr><tr><td>have</td><td>have not (haven&#x27;t)</td><td>□ I haven&#x27;t finished my work.</td></tr><tr><td>has</td><td>has not (hasn&#x27;t)</td><td>□ Sue hasn&#x27;t got a car.</td></tr><tr><td>will</td><td>will not (won&#x27;t)</td><td>□ We won&#x27;t be here tomorrow.</td></tr><tr><td>can</td><td>cannot (can&#x27;t)</td><td>□ George can&#x27;t drive.</td></tr><tr><td>could</td><td>could not (couldn&#x27;t)</td><td>□ I couldn&#x27;t sleep last night.</td></tr><tr><td>must</td><td>must not (mustn&#x27;t)</td><td>□ I mustn&#x27;t forget to phone Jane.</td></tr><tr><td>should</td><td>should not (shouldn&#x27;t)</td><td>□ You shouldn&#x27;t work so hard.</td></tr><tr><td>would</td><td>would not (wouldn&#x27;t)</td><td>□ I wouldn&#x27;t like to be an actor.</td></tr></table>

## don't/doesn't/didn't

<table><tr><td>一般现在时的否定式:</td><td>I/we/you/they do not (don&#x27;t) he/she/it does not (doesn&#x27;t)</td><td rowspan="2">work/live/go 等</td></tr><tr><td>一般过去时的否定式:</td><td>I/they/he/she 等 did not (didn&#x27;t)</td></tr></table>

<table><tr><td>I want to go out.</td><td>→</td><td>I don&#x27;t want to go out.</td></tr><tr><td>They work hard.</td><td>→</td><td>They don&#x27;t work hard.</td></tr><tr><td>Liz plays the guitar.</td><td>→</td><td>Liz doesn&#x27;t play the guitar.</td></tr><tr><td>My father likes his job.</td><td>→</td><td>My father doesn&#x27;t like his job.</td></tr><tr><td>I got up early this morning.</td><td>→</td><td>I didn&#x27;t get up early this morning.</td></tr><tr><td>They worked hard yesterday.</td><td>→</td><td>They didn&#x27;t work hard yesterday.</td></tr><tr><td>We played tennis.</td><td>→</td><td>We didn&#x27;t play tennis.</td></tr><tr><td>Diane had dinner with us.</td><td>→</td><td>Diane didn&#x27;t have dinner with us.</td></tr></table>

## Don't ...

<table><tr><td colspan="2">Look! → Don&#x27;t look!</td></tr><tr><td colspan="2">Wait for me. → Don&#x27;t wait for me.</td></tr></table>

do 有时可用作主动词，如 don't do / doesn't do / didn't do:

<table><tr><td>Do something!</td><td>→</td><td>Don’t do anything!</td></tr><tr><td>Sue does a lot at weekends.</td><td>→</td><td>Sue doesn’t do much at weekends.</td></tr><tr><td>I did what you said.</td><td>→</td><td>I didn’t do what you said.</td></tr></table>

## is it ... ? have you ... ? do they ... ? 等 (疑问句 1)

You are eating. 

疑问句：are you Are you eating? What are you eating?

疑问句中，第一个动词(is/are/have等）位于主语之前：

肯定句

疑问句

主语 + 谓语动词 谓语动词 + 主语

<table><tr><td>I</td><td>am late.</td><td>→</td><td>Am</td><td>I late?</td></tr><tr><td>That seat</td><td>is free.</td><td>→</td><td>Is</td><td>that seat free?</td></tr><tr><td>She</td><td>was angry.</td><td>→</td><td>Why was</td><td>she angry?</td></tr><tr><td>David</td><td>has gone.</td><td>→</td><td>Where has</td><td>David gone?</td></tr><tr><td>You</td><td>have got a car.</td><td>→</td><td>Have</td><td>you got a car?</td></tr><tr><td>They</td><td>will be here soon.</td><td>→</td><td>When will</td><td>they be here?</td></tr><tr><td>Paula</td><td>can swim.</td><td>→</td><td>Can</td><td>Paula swim?</td></tr></table>

注意，主语位于第一个动词之后：

□ Where has David gone? (而不用 Where has gone David?)

□ Are those people waiting for something? (而不用 Are waiting ... ?)

□ When was the telephone invented? (而不用 When was invented ... ?)

## do ... ? / does ... ? / did ... ?

<table><tr><td>do I/we/you/theydoes he/she/it</td><td rowspan="2">work/live/go 等...?</td></tr><tr><td>did I/they/he/she 等</td></tr></table>

<table><tr><td>肯定句</td><td>疑问句</td></tr><tr><td>Theyworkhard.</td><td><eq>\rightarrow</eq>Do they work hard?</td></tr><tr><td>Youwatchtelevision.</td><td><eq>\rightarrow</eq>How often do you watch television?</td></tr><tr><td>Chrisworkshard.</td><td><eq>\rightarrow</eq>Does Chris work hard?</td></tr><tr><td>Shegets upearly.</td><td><eq>\rightarrow</eq>What time does she get up?</td></tr><tr><td>Theyworkedhard.</td><td><eq>\rightarrow</eq>Did they work hard?</td></tr><tr><td>Youhaddinner.</td><td><eq>\rightarrow</eq>What did you have for dinner?</td></tr><tr><td>Shegotupearly.</td><td><eq>\rightarrow</eq>What time did she get up?</td></tr></table>

do 有时在句中作主动词 (do you do / did he do 等):

□ What do you usually do at weekends? 

□ 'What does your brother do?' 'He works in a bank.' 

□ 'I broke my finger last week.' 'How did you do that?' (而不用 How did you that?)

Why isn't ...? / Why don't ...? 等 (Why + 否定式):

□ Where's John? Why isn't he here? (而不用 Why he isn't here?)

□ Why can't Paula come to the meeting tomorrow? (而不用 Why Paula can't ... ?)

□ Why didn't you phone me last night? 

<table><tr><td>1 I can swim.</td><td>(and you?)</td><td>Can you swim?</td></tr><tr><td>2 I work hard.</td><td>(and Jack?)</td><td>Does Jack work hard?</td></tr><tr><td>3 I was late this morning.</td><td>(and you?)</td><td></td></tr><tr><td>4 I&#x27;ve got a key.</td><td>(and Kate?)</td><td></td></tr><tr><td>5 I&#x27;ll be here tomorrow.</td><td>(and you?)</td><td></td></tr><tr><td>6 I&#x27;m going out this evening.</td><td>(and Paul?)</td><td></td></tr><tr><td>7 I like my job.</td><td>(and you?)</td><td></td></tr><tr><td>8 I live near here.</td><td>(and Nicole?)</td><td></td></tr><tr><td>9 I enjoyed the film.</td><td>(and you?)</td><td></td></tr><tr><td>10 I had a good holiday.</td><td>(and you?)</td><td></td></tr></table>

## Unit 45

## Who saw you? Who did you see? (疑问句 2)

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/fa87606b58e36a83.jpg)


在下列疑问句中，who/what 是主语：
□ Who lives in this house? (= somebody lives in it - who?)
(而不用 Who does live?)
□ What happened? (= something happened - what?)
(而不用 What did happen?)
□ What's happening? (What's = What is)
□ Who's got my key? (Who's = Who has)

在下列疑问句中，who/what 是宾语：
□ Who did you meet yesterday? (= you met somebody - who?)
□ What did Paul say? (= Paul said something - what?)
□ Who are you phoning?
□ What was Silvia wearing?

请比较：
□ George likes oranges. → Who likes oranges? – George.
What does George like? – Oranges.
□ Jane won a new car. → Who won a new car? – Jane.
What did Jane win? – A new car.

who 指代人，what 指代事物、想法等：
□ Who is your favourite singer?
□ What is your favourite song?

## 45.1 用 who 或 what（作主语）提问。

Somebody broke the window. Something fell off the shelf. Somebody wants to see you. Somebody took my umbrella. Something made me ill. Somebody is coming. 

Who broke the window?
What 

## 45.2 用 who 或 what（作主语或宾语）提问。

I bought something.
Somebody lives in this house.
I phoned somebody.
Something happened last night.
Somebody knows the answer.
Somebody did the washing-up.
Jane did something.
Something woke me up.
Somebody saw the accident.
I saw somebody.
Somebody has got my pen.
This word means something. 

What did you buy?
Who lives in this house? 

## 45.3 你想知道XXXX 处缺失的信息。用 who 或 what 提问。

I lost XXXXX yesterday, but fortunately
XXXXX found it and gave it back to me. 

XXXXX phoned me last night. She wanted
XXXXX. 

What did you lose?
Who found it? 

I needed some advice, so I asked XXXXX. He said XXXXX. 

Who . What 

I hear that XXXXX got married last week.
XXXXX told me. 

I met XXXXX on my way home this evening. She told me XXXXX. 

Steve and I played tennis yesterday.
XXXXX won. After the game we XXXXX. 

It was my birthday last week and I had some presents. XXXXX gave me a book and Catherine gave me XXXXX. 

## Who is she talking to? What is it like? (疑问句 3)

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/0184c01a2604ced7.jpg)


Julia is talking to somebody. 

Who is she talking to? 

以 Who ... ? / What ... ? / Where ... ? / Which ... ? 开头的疑问句中，介词 (to/from/with 等) 常位于句尾：

□ 'Where are you from?' 'I'm from Thailand.' 

□ 'Jack was afraid.' 'What was he afraid of?' 

□ 'Who do these books belong to?' 'They're mine.' 

□ 'Tom's father is in hospital.' 'Which hospital is he in?' 

□ 'Kate is going on holiday.' 'Who with?' / 'Who is she going with?' 

□ 'Can we talk?' 'Sure. What do you want to talk about?' 

## What's it like? / What are they like? 等

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/9fab7442fba528d2.jpg)


What's it like? = What is it like? 

What's it like? 表示询问某事物的情况——好坏、大小、新旧等。

What is it like? 中的 like 是介词，而不是动词 like (Do you like your new house? 等):

□ A: There's a new restaurant in our street. 

B: What's it like? Is it good? 

A: I don't know. I haven't eaten there yet. 

A: What's your new teacher like? B: She's very good. We learn a lot. 

□ A: I met Nicole's parents yesterday. 

B: Did you? What are they like? 

A: They're very nice. 

□ A: Did you have a good holiday? What was the weather like? 

B: It was lovely. It was sunny every day. 

## Exercises

The letter is from XXXXX. 

Who is the letter from? 

I'm looking for a XXXXX. 

What 

I went to the cinema with XXXXX. 

The film was about XXXXX.

The book was written by XXXXX.

## Unit 47

## What ...? (疑问句 4)

## Which ... ? How ... ?

what + 名词 (What colour ... ? / What kind ... ? 等)

□ What colour is your car? 

□ What colour are your eyes? 

□ What size is this shirt? 

□ What make is your TV set? 

□ What time is it? 

□ What day is it today? 

□ What kind of job do you want? (或 What type of job ... ? / What sort of job ... ?)

what 后可不带名词：

□ What's your favourite colour? 

□ What do you want to do tonight? 

## which + 名词（物或人）:

□ Which train did you catch – the 9.50 or the 10.30? 

□ Which doctor did you see – Doctor Ellis, Doctor Gray or Doctor Hill? 

which 后不带名词时指代物，不指代人：

□ Which is bigger – Canada or Australia? 

who 指代人，后面不带名词：

□ Who is taller – Joe or Gary? (而不用 Which is taller?)

## what 与 which 比较

which 表示可能的选择较少（或许有 2 个、3 个或 4 个选择）：

□ We can go this way or that way. 

Which way shall we go? 

☐ There are four umbrellas here.
Which is yours? 

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/e469dd8a1fea8f8d.jpg)


what 表示的范围则更广：

WHICH? 

□ What's the capital of Argentina? (在阿根廷的所有城市中)

□ What sort of music do you like? (在所有种类的音乐中)

请比较：

□ What colour are his eyes? (而不用 Which colour?)

Which colour do you prefer, pink or yellow? 

□ What is the longest river in the world? 

Which is the longest river – the Mississippi, the Amazon or the Nile? 

## How ...?

□ 'How was the party last night?' 'It was great.' 

□ 'How do you usually go to work?' 'By bus.' 

可以用 how + 形容词 / 副词 (how tall / how old / how often 等):

<table><tr><td>‘How</td><td>tall are you?’ ‘I’m 1 metre 70.’big is the house?’ ‘Not very big.’old is your mother?’ ‘She’s 45.’far is it from here to the airport?’ ‘Five kilometres.’often do you use your car?’ ‘Every day.’long have they been married?’ ‘Ten years.’much was the meal?’ ‘Thirty pounds.’</td></tr></table>

## How long does it take from ... to ... ?

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/e7530c3aaae149e3.jpg)


How long does it take by plane from New York to Washington? 

It takes an hour. 

□ How long does it take by train from London to Manchester?
□ It takes two hours by train from London to Manchester.
□ How long does it take by car from your house to the station?
□ It takes ten minutes by car from my house to the station. 

## How long does it take to do something?

<table><tr><td rowspan="2">It</td><td colspan="2">takestookwill take</td><td>a weeka long timethree hours</td><td rowspan="2">to ...</td></tr><tr><td>doesn’tdidn’twon’t</td><td>take</td><td>long</td></tr></table>

□ How long does it take to cross the Atlantic by ship?
□ 'I came by train.' 'Did you? How long did it take (to get here)?'
□ How long will it take to get from here to the hotel?
□ It takes a long time to learn a language.
□ It doesn't take long to cook an omelette.
□ It won't take long to fix the computer. 

## How long does it take you to do something?

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/88f2c5aab1ab2aa6.jpg)


<table><tr><td>How long</td><td>doesdidwill</td><td>it take</td><td>youTomthem</td><td>to ... ?</td></tr></table>

<table><tr><td>It</td><td>takestookwill take</td><td>meTomthem</td><td>a weeka long timethree hours</td><td>to ...</td></tr></table>

I started reading the book on Monday. I finished it on Wednesday evening. 

It took me three days to read it. 

□ How long will it take me to learn to drive?
□ It takes Tom 20 minutes to get to work in the morning.
□ It took us an hour to do the shopping.
□ Did it take you a long time to find a job?
□ It will take me an hour to cook dinner.

# Do you know where ...? I don't know what ... 等

Do you know
where Paula is? 

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/e69594f6d05a9025.jpg)


可以说： Where is Paula?

可以说：Do you know where Paula is? (而不用 Do you know where is Paula?)

同样可以说：

I know
I don't know} where Paula is.
Can you tell me where Paula is?

## 带有 do/does/did 的疑问句（一般现在时与一般过去时）

## Where does he live?

或 Do you know where he lives? (而不用 Do you know where does he live?)

请比较：

<table><tr><td>Do you know</td><td rowspan="2">how aeroplanes flywhat Jane wantswhy she went homewhere I put the key</td><td>?</td></tr><tr><td>I don&#x27;t knowI don&#x27;t rememberI know</td><td>.</td></tr></table>

## C Is ...? / Do ...? / Can ...? 等句式的疑问句（一般疑问句）:

## 请比较：

<table><tr><td>Do you know</td><td rowspan="2">if或whether</td><td rowspan="2">Jack is at homethey&#x27;ve got a carBrian can swimthey live near hereanybody saw you</td><td>?</td></tr><tr><td>I don&#x27;t know</td><td>.</td></tr></table>

if 或 whether 可用于下列句子中：

□ Do you know if they've got a car? 或 Do you know whether they've got a car?
□ I don't know if anybody saw me. 或 I don't know whether anybody saw me.

## She said that ... He told me that ...

上周你去参加一个聚会，许多朋友在那儿。如下是他们对你所说的话：

你今天遇到了保罗，对他说了聚会的事。如下是你向保罗转述朋友们所说的话：

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/049ac0433131fe3c.jpg)


<table><tr><td colspan="2">say 与 tell 比较:</td></tr><tr><td>say (→ said)□ He said that he was tired.(而不用 He said me)□ What did she say to you?(而不用 say you)可以说 he said to me, I said to Ann 等,但不可以说 he said me, I said Ann。</td><td>tell (→ told)□ He told me that he was tired.(而不用 He told that)□ What did she tell you?(而不用 tell to you)可以说 he told me, I told Ann 等,但不可以说 he told to me, I told to Ann。</td></tr></table>

## work/working go/going do/doing

## work/go/be 等（动词原形）

## will/can/must 等后接动词原形：

will 

□ Anna will be here soon. 

shall 

□ Shall I open the window? 

→ 参见 Units 27-28

might □ I might phone you later. 

may □ May I sit here? 

→ 参见 Unit 29

can □ I can't meet you tomorrow. 

could □ Could you pass the salt, please? 

→ 参见 Unit 30

must □ It's late. I must go now. 

should □ You shouldn't work so hard. → 参见 Unit 32

→ 参见 Unit 31

would □ Would you like some coffee? → 参见 Unit 34

## do/does/did 后接动词原形：

## do/does

(一般现在时)

□ Do you work? 

□ They don't work very hard. 

→ 参见 Units 6-7

□ Helen doesn't know many people. 

□ How much does it cost? 

did 

(一般过去时)

□ What time did the train leave? → 参见 Unit 12

□ We didn't sleep well. 

## to work / to go / to be 等 (to + 动词原形)

(I'm) going to ... 

□ I'm going to play tennis tomorrow. → 参见 Unit 26

□ What are you going to do? 

(I) have to ... 

□ I have to go now. → 参见 Unit 33

□ Everybody has to eat. 

(I) want to ... 

□ Do you want to go out? → 参见 Unit 52

□ They don't want to come with us. 

(I) would like to ... 

□ I'd like to talk to you. → 参见 Unit 34

□ Would you like to go out? 

(I) used to ... 

□ Dave used to work in a factory. → 参见 Unit 36

## working/going/playing 等（现在分词）

## am/is/are + -ing (现在进行时)

□ Please be quiet. I'm working. → 参见 Units 3-4, 8, 25

□ Tom isn't working today. 

□ What time are you going out? 

was/were+ -ing 

(过去进行时)

□ It was raining, so we didn't go out. → 参见 Units 13-14

□ What were you doing when the phone rang?

## 51.3 用动词的适当形式填空：动词原形（work/go 等），带 to 的动词不定式（to work / to go 等）

或动词 -ing 形式 (working/going 等)。

1 Shall I open the window? (open) 

3 Amanda isn't working this week. She's on holiday. (work) 

4 I'm tired. I don't want .... out. (go) 

5 It might ____, so take an umbrella with you. (rain) 

6 What time do you have ____ tomorrow morning? (leave) 

7 I'm sorry I can't you. (help) 

8 My brother is a student. He's ____ physics. (study) 

9 Would you like ____ on a trip round the world? (go) 

10 When you saw Maria, what was she ____? (wear) 

11 When you go to London, where are you going ____? (stay) 

12 I'm hungry. I must ____ something to eat. (have) 

13 'Where's Gary?' 'He's a bath.' (have) 

14 I used ____ a car, but I sold it last year. (have) 

15 He spoke very quietly. I couldn't him. (hear) 

16 You don't look well. I don't think you should ____ to work today. (go) 

17 I don't know what he said. I wasn't ____ to him. (listen) 

18 I'm sorry I'm late. I had a phone call. (make) 

19 I want .... what happened. (know) You must .... me. (tell) 

20 May I ____ your phone? (use) 

# 动词不定式（I want to do）与 -ing 形式（I enjoy doing）比较

## 动词 + 不定式 (I want to do)

want plan 

decide try 

hope expect 

need promise 

+ to ... (to do / to work / to be 等)

□ What do you want to do this evening? 

□ It's not very late. We don't need to go home yet. 

□ Tina has decided to sell her car. 

☐ You forgot to switch off the light when you went out. 

□ My brother is learning to drive. 

□ I tried to read my book, but I was too tired. 

## B 动词 + -ing 形式 (I enjoy doing)

suggest 

+ -ing (doing / working / being 等)

□ I enjoy dancing. (而不用 enjoy to dance)

□ I don't mind getting up early. 

□ Has it stopped raining? 

□ Sonia suggested going to the cinema. 

I enjoy dancing. 

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/49ec41c31319917d.jpg)


## 动词 + -ing 形式或不定式

continue 

+ -ing (doing 等) 或 to ... (to do 等)

□ Do you like getting up early? 或 Do you like to get up early?

□ I prefer travelling by car. 或 I prefer to travel by car.

□ Anna loves dancing. 或 Anna loves to dance.

□ I hate being late. 或 I hate to be late.

□ It started raining. 或 It started to rain.

## D would like to ... 等

+ to ... (to do / to work / to be 等)

□ Julia would like to meet you. 

□ I'd love to go to Australia. (I'd = I would) 

□ 'Would you like to sit down?' 'No, I'd prefer to stand, thank you.' 

□ I like this city very much. I wouldn't like to move. 

□ I'd hate to lose my address book. 

## Exercises

## 52.1 用动词的不定式（to ...) 或 -ing 形式填空。

1 I enjoy ____ dancing ____. (dance) 

2 What do you want to do tonight? (do) 

3 Bye! I hope .... you again soon. (see) 

4 I learnt ____ when I was five years old. (swim) 

5 Have you finished the kitchen? (clean) 

6 Where's Anna? I need her something. (ask) 

8 The weather was nice, so I suggested ____ for a walk by the river. (go) 

9 Where's Bill? He promised .....
here on time. (be) 

10 I'm not in a hurry. I don't mind ____. (wait) 

11 What have you decided ....? (do) 

12 Gary was very angry and refused to me. (speak) 

13 I'm tired. I want to bed. (go) 

14 I was very upset and started .... (cry) 

7 Do you enjoy ____ other countries? (visit) 15 I'm trying ____. (work) Please stop ____. (talk)

## I want you to ... I told you to ...

## I want you to

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/5c23fff98d8855f4.jpg)


The woman wants to go. 

The man doesn't want the woman to go. He wants her to stay. 

可以说：

<table><tr><td>I want</td><td>yousomebodySarah</td><td>to do something</td></tr></table>

□ I want you to be happy. (而不用 I want that you are happy)

□ They didn't want anybody to know their secret. 

□ Do you want me to lend you some money? 

同样可以用 would like:

□ Would you like me to lend you some money? 

## 动词 + somebody + to ... 结构：

<table><tr><td></td><td colspan="2">动词 +</td><td colspan="3">somebody + to ...</td></tr><tr><td>ask</td><td>Sue</td><td>asked</td><td>a friend</td><td>to lend</td><td>her some money.</td></tr><tr><td>tell</td><td>I</td><td>told</td><td>you</td><td>to be</td><td>careful.</td></tr><tr><td>advise</td><td>What do you</td><td>advise</td><td>me</td><td>to do?</td><td></td></tr><tr><td>expect</td><td>I didn&#x27;t</td><td>expect</td><td>them</td><td>to be</td><td>here.</td></tr><tr><td>persuade</td><td>We</td><td>persuaded</td><td>Gary</td><td>to come</td><td>with us.</td></tr><tr><td>teach</td><td>I</td><td>am teaching</td><td>my brother</td><td>to swim.</td><td></td></tr></table>

## make 与 let 的用法

在 make 和 let 后面，不可使用 to:

□ He's very funny. He makes me laugh. (而不用 makes me to laugh)

□ At school our teacher made us work very hard. 

□ Sue let me use her computer because mine wasn't working. (而不用 let me to use)

当想要某人与你一起做某事时，可以用 Let's ... (= Let us):

□ Come on! Let's dance. 

□ 'Do you want to go out tonight?' 'No, I'm tired. Let's stay at home.' 

Let's ... → Unit 35 He told me that ... → Unit 50

## Unit 54

## I went to the shop to ...

## NEWSPAPERS

Paula wanted a newspaper, so she went to the shop. 

Why did she go to the shop?
To get a newspaper. 

或

She went to the shop to get a newspaper. 

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/66fff11159ad9b2e.jpg)


to ... (to get / to see 等) 表示某人为什么做某事:

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/67a091e33d3f67b5.jpg)


## NEWSPAPERS

□ 'Why are you going out?' 'To get some bread.' 

□ Catherine went to the station to meet her friend. 

□ Sue turned on the television to watch the news. 

□ I'd like to go to Spain to learn Spanish. 

money/time to (do something): 

□ We need some money to buy food. 

□ I haven't got time to watch television. 

## to ... 与 for ... 比较

to + 动词

(to get / to see 等)

□ I went to the shop to get a newspaper.
(而不用 for get)

□ They're going to Brazil to see their friends. 

□ We need some money to buy food. 

for + 名词

(for a newspaper / for food 等)

□ I went to the shop for a newspaper. 

□ They're going to Brazil for a holiday. 

□ We need some money for food. 

## wait for ...:

□ Please wait for me. 

□ Are you waiting for the bus? 

wait to (do something): 

□ Hurry up! I'm waiting to go. 

□ Are you waiting to see the doctor? 

wait for (somebody/something) to ...: 

□ I can't go out yet. I'm waiting for John to phone. 

□ Are you waiting for the doctor to come? 

I can't go out yet. I'm waiting for John to phone. 

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/b9780fed8784ecb5.jpg)

## Unit 55

## go to ... go on ... go for ... go -ing

## go to ... (go to work / go to London / go to a concert 等)

□ What time do you usually go to work? 

□ I'm going to China next week. 

□ Sophie didn't want to go to the concert. 

□ 'Where's Tom?' 'He's gone to bed.' 

□ I went to the dentist yesterday. 

go to 

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/521ff4d6d4becc9a.jpg)


## go to sleep 表示 “入睡”

□ I was very tired and went to sleep quickly. 

go home (不带 to) 表示 “回家”：

□ I'm going home now. (而不用 going to home)

## go on ...

<table><tr><td>go on</td><td>holidaya tripa touran excursiona cruisestrike</td></tr></table>

□ We're going on holiday next week. 

□ Children often go on school trips. 

□ When we were in Scotland, we went on a lot of excursions to different places. 

□ Workers at the airport have gone on strike. (= they are refusing to work) 

## go for ...

<table><tr><td>go (somewhere) for</td><td>a walk a run a swim a drink a meal</td></tr></table>

□ 'Where's Emma?' 'She's gone for a walk.' 

□ Do you go for a run every morning? 

□ The water looks nice. I'm going for a swim. 

□ I met Chris in town, so we went for a coffee. 

□ Shall we go out for a meal? I know a good restaurant. 

## go -ing

## go -ing 可表示进行体育活动 (swimming / skiing 等) 或去购物 (shopping):

<table><tr><td>I gohe is goingwe wentthey have goneshe wants to go</td><td>shoppingswimmingfishingsailingskiingjogging 等</td></tr></table>

□ Are you going shopping this afternoon? 

□ It's a nice day. Let's go swimming.
(或 Let's go for a swim.)

☐ Richard has a small boat and he often goes sailing. 

□ I went jogging before breakfast this morning.

get on 

get 后接名词 (get a letter / get a job 等) 时表示 “收到 / 买到 / 找到某物”：

you get it 

you don't have something 

you have it 

- 'Did you get my postcard?' 'Yes, I got it yesterday.' (= receive)
- I like your sweater. Where did you get it? (= buy)
- Is it difficult to get a job at the moment? (= find)
- (on the phone) 'Hello, can I speak to Lisa, please?' 'Sure. I'll get her.' 

此外还有 get a bus / a train / a taxi（乘公共汽车 / 火车 / 出租车）：□ 'Did you walk here?' 'No, I got the bus.'

## get 后接形容词 (get hungry / get cold / get tired 等) 时表示 “变得”：

you get hungry 

you're not hungry 

you are hungry 

□ If you don't eat, you get hungry.
□ Drink your coffee. It's getting cold.
□ I'm sorry your mother is ill. I hope she gets better soon.
□ It was raining very hard. We didn't have an umbrella, so we got very wet. 

此外还有：get married（结婚）
get dressed（穿衣）
get lost（迷路）

- Nicole and Frank are getting married soon.
- I got up and got dressed quickly.
- We didn't have a map, so we got lost. 

## get to 后接地点时表示 “到达”

☐ I usually get to work before 8.30. (= arrive at work)
☐ We left London at 10 o'clock and got to Manchester at 12.45. 

get here/there (不带 to):
□ How did you get here? By bus?

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/8d5394bf312f5c4a.jpg)


get home (不带 to) 表示 “到家”：
□ What time did you get home last night?

## get in/out/on/off

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/1963e404039014ac.jpg)



get in (a car)



get out (of a car)



get off



(a bus / a train / a plane)


- Kate got in the car and drove away. (也可说: Kate got into the car and ...)
- A car stopped and a man got out. (也可说: A man got out of the car.)
- We got on the bus outside the hotel and got off in Church Street.

## Unit 57

## do 与 make 比较

## do 是表示动作的常用词：

□ What are you doing this evening? (而不用 What are you making?)

□ 'Shall I open the window?' 'No, it's OK. I'll do it.' 

□ Rachel's job is very boring. She does the same thing every day. 

□ I did a lot of things yesterday. 

What do you do? 表示询问对方的职业：

□ 'What do you do?' 'I work in a bank.' 

## make 表示 “生产 / 制作”：

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/944e0898c787c7e7.jpg)


She's making coffee. He has made a cake. They make umbrellas. It was made in China. 

请比较 do 与 make:

□ I did a lot yesterday. I cleaned my room, I wrote some letters and I made a cake. 

□ A: What do you do in your free time? Sport? Reading? Hobbies? 

B: I make clothes. I make dresses and jackets. I also make toys for my children. 

## C

## do 构成的短语

<table><tr><td>do</td><td>an exam / a testa coursehomeworkhouseworksomebody a favouran exercise</td><td>□ I&#x27;m doing my driving test next week.□ John has just done a training course.□ Our children have to do a lot of homework.□ I hate doing housework, especially cleaning.□ Sue, could you do me a favour?□ I go for a run and do exercises every morning.</td></tr></table>

还有 do the shopping / do the washing / do the washing-up / do the ironing / do the cooking 等：

□ I did the washing, but I didn't do the shopping. 

## make 构成的短语

拍电影用 make a film，拍照用 take a photograph:

□ When was this film made? 但必须说 When was this photograph taken?

1 He's making a cake. 6   
2 They 7   
3 He 8   
4 9   
5 10

## Unit 58

## have

## have 与 have got 比较

I've got (something) 或 I have (something) 表示 “某物是我的”：
□ I've got a new car. 或 I have a new car.
□ Sue has got long hair. 或 Sue has long hair.
□ Have they got any children? 或 Do they have any children?
□ Tim hasn't got a job. 或 Tim doesn't have a job.
□ How much time have you got? 或 How much time do you have?

此外还有：

I've got } a headache / (a) toothache / a pain (in my leg 等)
I have a cold / a cough / a sore throat / a temperature / flu 等

□ I've got a headache. 或 I have a headache.
□ Have you got a cold? 或 Do you have a cold?

过去时为 I had (无 got) / I didn't have / Did you have? 等：
□ When I first met Sue, she had short hair.
□ He didn't have any money because he didn't have a job.
□ Did you have enough time to do everything you wanted?

## B have breakfast / have a shower 等

这些短语中的 have 表示 “吃、喝、拿等”。不可用 have got 代替：

breakfast / lunch / dinner
a meal / a sandwich / a pizza 等
a cup of coffee / a glass of milk 等
something to eat/drink

在下列短语中，要用 have（而不用 have got）：

have
a bath / a shower
a rest / a holiday / a party
a nice time / a good trip / fun 等
a walk / a swim / a game (of tennis 等)
a dream / an accident
a baby
a look (at something)

## 请比较：

have got 或 have

□ I've got / I have a new shower. It's very good. 

have (而不用 have got)

□ I have a shower every morning.
(而不用 I've got a shower every morning)

□ A: Where's Paul? 

B: He's having a shower. (= he's washing now) 

□ 'Where's Liz?' 'She's having lunch.' 

□ I don't usually have breakfast. 

☐ I had three cups of coffee this morning. 

□ 'Have a biscuit!' 'Oh, thank you.' 

□ I had a shower this morning. 

□ We're having a party next week. You must come. 

□ Enjoy your holiday. Have a nice time! 

□ Did you have a good time in Tokyo? 

□ Sandra has just had a baby. 

□ Can I have a look at your newspaper? 

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/54a44c90073908a6.jpg)


## Exercises

## 58.1 用 have 或 have got 的适当形式填空。

1 I didn't have time to do the shopping yesterday. (I / not / have) 

2 'Has Lisa got (OR Does Lisa have) a car?' 'No, she can't drive.' (Lisa / have?) 

3. He can't open the door. ____ a key. (he / not / have) 

4 a cold last week. He's better now. (Gary / have) 

5 What's wrong? a headache? (you / have?) 

6 We wanted to go by taxi, but .... enough money. (we / not / have) 

7 Liz is very busy. ____ much free time. (she / not / have) 

8 ____ any problems when you were on holiday? (you / have?) 

## 58.2 下列图片中的人物正在做什么？用所给词语完成句子。

## 58.3 在下列情形中你会说什么？用 have 造句。

1 Emily is going on holiday. What do you say to her before she goes? Have a nice holiday! 

2 You meet Claire at the airport. She has just got off her plane. Ask her about the flight. Did you have a good flight? 

3 Tim is going on a long trip. What do you say to him before he leaves? 

4 It's Monday morning. You are at work. Ask Paula about her weekend. 

5 Paul has just come home after playing tennis with a friend. Ask him about the game. 

6 Rachel is going out this evening. What do you say to her before she goes? 

7 Mark has just returned from holiday. Ask him about his holiday.

3 I was thirsty, so I ____ .

5 Tina is a very good driver. She has never ____ . 

6 There's something wrong with the engine of my car. Can you ____ at it?

he

they them


主语
I I know Tom.
we We know Tom.
you You know Tom.
he He knows Tom.
she She knows Tom.
they They know Tom.

Tom knows me. me
Tom knows us. us
Tom knows you. you
Tom knows him. him
Tom knows her. her
Tom knows them. them 

## 物体

It's nice. I like it. 

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/90c887d686020adb.jpg)


They're nice. I like them. 

it 

□ I don't want this book. You can have it.
□ I don't want these books. You can have them.
□ Diane never drinks milk. She doesn't like it.
□ I never go to parties. I don't like them. 

me/her/them 等宾格代词用于介词 (for/to/with 等) 之后：
□ This letter isn't for me. It's for you.
□ Who is that woman? Why are you looking at her?
□ We're going to the cinema. Do you want to come with us?
□ Sue and Kevin are going to the cinema. Do you want to go with them?
□ 'Where's the newspaper?' 'You're sitting on it.'

give it/them to ... 中的 it/them 为直接宾语，直接跟在主动词之后，间接宾语之前则要加 to:
□ I want that book. Please give it to me.
□ Robert needs these books. Can you give them to him, please?

59.1 用 him/her/them 完成句子。
1 I don't know those girls. Do you know ____ ? 
2 I don't know that man. Do you know ____ ? 
3 I don't know those people. Do you know ____ ? 
4 I don't know David's wife. Do you know ____ ? 
5 I don't know Mr Stevens. Do you know ____ ? 
6 I don't know Sarah's parents. Do you know ____ ? 
7 I don't know the woman in the black coat. Do you know ____ ? 

59.2 用 l/me/you/she/her 等完成句子。
1 I want to see her, but ____ doesn't want to see me ____. 
2 They want to see me, but ____ don't want to see ____. 
3 She wants to see him, but ____ doesn't want to see ____. 
4 We want to see them, but ____ don't want to see ____. 
5 He wants to see us, but ____ don't want to see ____. 
6 They want to see her, but ____ doesn't want to see ____. 
7 I want to see them, but ____ don't want to see ____. 
8 You want to see her, but ____ doesn't want to see ____.

3 This jacket isn't very nice. I don't ____. 
4 This is my new car. Do ____ ?

6 These are my new shoes. ____ ?

## my/his/their 等

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/0099eff9fbf6cbd3.jpg)


my umbrella 

our umbrella 

your umbrella 

his umbrella 

her umbrella 

their umbrella 

I → my 

I like my house. 

we → our 

We like our house. 

you → your 

You like your house. 

he → his 

He likes his house. 

she → her 

She likes her house. 

they → their 

They like their house. 

it $\rightarrow$ its 

Oxford (= It) is famous for its university. 

## my/your/his 等 + 名词：

my hands 

his new car 

our clothes 

your best friend 

her parents 

their room

## its 与 it's 比较

Oxford is famous for its university. 

it's (= it is) I like Oxford. It's a nice place. (= It is a nice place.)

## Unit 61

## Whose is this? It's mine/yours/hers 等

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/344c5eb433d2f837.jpg)


![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/d6ec943d0e5ec9a9.jpg)


![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/1f83d0217727d19c.jpg)


![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/e820c5694c0a20ec.jpg)


![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/5a6c3b26261e9e61.jpg)


![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/277a541c7cc850db.jpg)


I → my → mine 

we → our → ours 

you → your → yours 

he → his → his 

she → her → hers 

they → their → theirs 

It's my money. 

It's mine. 

It's our money. It's ours. 

It's his money. It's his. 

It's her money. It's hers. 

It's their money. It's theirs. 

## my/your 等 + 名词 (my hands / your book 等):

□ My hands are cold. 

□ Is this your book? 

□ Helen gave me her umbrella. 

□ It's their problem, not our problem. 

## mine/yours 等后面不跟名词：

□ Is this book mine or yours? (= my book or your book) 

□ I didn't have an umbrella, so Helen gave me hers. (= her umbrella) 

□ It's their problem, not ours. (= not our problem) 

☐ We went in our car, and they went in theirs. (= their car) 

## his 后带不带名词均可：

□ 'Is this his camera or hers?' 'It's his.' 

## a friend of mine / a friend of his / some friends of yours 等

□ I went out to meet a friend of mine. (而不用 a friend of me)

□ Tom was in the restaurant with a friend of his. (而不用 a friend of him)

□ Are those people friends of yours? (而不用 friends of you)

## Whose ... ?

□ Whose book is this? (= Is it your book? his book? my book? 等)

## whose 之后带不带名词均可：

□ Whose money is this? 

Whose is this? 

□ Whose shoes are these? 

Whose are these? 

It's mine. 

They're John's. 

NOTEBOOK 

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/6ae8c973ff1f7281.jpg)


61.1 用 mine/yours 等完成句子。
1 It's your money. It's yours....5 It's their house. It's .....
2 It's my bag. It's ....6 They're your books. They're .....
3 It's our car. It's ....7 They're my glasses. They're .....
4 They're her shoes. They're ....8 It's his coat. It's ....

1 It's their/theirs problem, not our/ours. (their and ours are right)
2 This is a nice camera. Is it your/yours?
3 That's not my/mine umbrella. My/Mine is black.
4 Whose books are these? Your/Yours or my/mine?
5 Catherine is going out with her/hers friends this evening.
6 My/Mine room is bigger than her/hers.
7 They've got two children, but I don't know their/theirs names.
8 Can we use your washing machine? Our/Ours isn't working.

1 I went to the cinema with a ____ friend of mine
2 They went on holiday with some ____ friends of theirs
3 She's going out with a friend
4 We had dinner with some
5 I played tennis with a
6 Tom is going to meet a
7 Do you know those people? Are they

## I/me/my/mine

## 请看下列例句：

□ 'Do you know that man?' 'Yes, I know him, but I can't remember his name.' 

☐ She was very pleased because we invited her to stay with us at our house. 

□ A: Where are the children? Have you seen them? 

B: Yes, they are playing with their friends in the park. 

□ That's my pen. Can you give it to me, please? 

□ 'Is this your umbrella?' 'No, it's yours.' 

□ He didn't have an umbrella, so she gave him hers. (= she gave her umbrella to him) 

□ I'm going out with a friend of mine this evening. (而不用 a friend of me)

myself/yourself 等 → Unit 63 Give me that book! / Give it to me! → Unit 96

## myself/yourself/themselves 等

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/f85d457ff6e82eb4.jpg)

## He's looking at himself.

I → me → myself 

he → him → himself 

she → her → herself 

you → you 

yourself 

we → us 

yourselves 

ourselves 

they → them → themselves 

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/1d6d924739f7c68d.jpg)



They're enjoying themselves.


□ I looked at myself in the mirror. 

□ He cut himself with a knife. 

□ She fell off her bike, but she didn't hurt herself. 

□ Please help yourself. (一个人)

□ Please help yourselves. (两个或两个以上的人)

□ We had a good holiday. We enjoyed ourselves. 

□ They had a nice time. They enjoyed themselves.

## by myself / by yourself 等表示 “独自”：

☐ I went on holiday by myself. (= I went alone) 

□ 'Was she with friends?' 'No, she was by herself.' 

## each other

(= Kate knows Helen / Helen knows Kate) 

□ Paul and I live near each other. (= he lives near me / I live near him)

## -'s (Kate's camera / my brother's car 等)

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/dc906ce19633df36.jpg)



Kate's camera (her camera)


![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/d846ad4c0ea13b5c.jpg)



my brother's car (his car)


![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/861ac1844dfdf946.jpg)



the manager's office (his 或 her office)


-’s 通常用于人：
□ I stayed at my sister's house. (而不用 the house of my sister)
□ Have you met Mr Black's wife? (而不用 the wife of Mr Black)
□ Are you going to James's party?
□ Paul is a man's name. Paula is a woman's name.

-’s 后不一定带有名词：
□ Sophie's hair is longer than Kate's. (= Kate's hair)
□ ‘Whose umbrella is this?’ ‘It's my mother's.’ (= my mother's umbrella)
□ ‘Where were you last night?’ ‘I was at Paul's.’ (= Paul's house)

## friend's 与 friends' 比较：

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/00dc6f5c77aeebf0.jpg)


my friend's house 一个朋友的房子 (= his house or her house)

's 用于 friend/student/mother 等（单数）之后：

my mother's car (母亲一个人)
my father's car (父亲一个人)

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/cc27522b22c0faa9.jpg)



my friends' house 两个或多个朋友的房子 (= their house)



'用于 friends/students/parents 等（复数）
之后：
my parents' car（父母亲两个人）


of ... 用于物体、地点等：

- Look at the roof of that building. (而不用 that building's roof)
- We didn't see the beginning of the film. (而不用 the film's beginning)
- What's the name of this village?
- Do you know the cause of the problem?
- You can sit in the back of the car.
- Madrid is the capital of Spain.

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/18d92c07873fc3ae.jpg)


They have a son, James, and a daughter, Sarah. 

Sarah is married to Paul. 

1 Brian is Helen's husband. 

2 Sarah is Daniel's mother. 

3 Helen is ____ wife. 

4 James is Sarah's 

5 James is .... uncle. 

6 Sarah is ____ wife. 

7 Helen is Daniel's 

Sarah and Paul have a son, Daniel. 

8 Sarah is James's 

9 Paul is ____ husband. 

10 Paul is Daniel's 

11 Daniel is ____ nephew.

## 64.3 判断下列句子的对错。如有错误，请改正。

1 I stayed at the house of my sister. 

2 What is the name of this village? 

my sister's house 

3 Do you like the colour of this coat? 

4 Do you know the phone number of Simon? 

5 The job of my brother is very interesting. 

6 Write your name at the top of the page. 

7 For me, the morning is the best part of the day. 

8 The favourite colour of Paula is blue. 

9 When is the birthday of your mother? 

10 The house of my parents isn't very big. 

11 The walls of this house are very thin. 

12 The car stopped at the end of the street. 

13 Are you going to the party of Silvia next week? 

14 The manager of the hotel is not here at the moment. 

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/42f87bcc2dd9a5d8.jpg)


He's got a camera. 

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/35b243cb3c0dde22.jpg)



She's waiting for a taxi.


![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/5b2c352322512122.jpg)



It's a beautiful day.


a ... 表示 “一个（事物或人）”：
□ Rachel works in a bank. (而不用 in bank)
□ Can I ask a question? (而不用 ask question)
□ I haven't got a computer.
□ There's a woman at the bus stop.

元音 a/e/i/o/u 前用 an (而不用 a):
□ Do you want an apple or a banana?
□ I'm going to buy a hat and an umbrella.
□ There was an interesting programme on TV last night.

要说 an hour（因为 h 不发音）
a university（因为 university 的读音以辅音开头）
a European country（因为 European 的读音以辅音开头）

another (= an + other) 是一个词：
□ Can I have another cup of coffee?

介绍某事物或某人时，要用 a/an ...:
□ The sun is a star.
□ Football is a game.
□ Dallas is a city in Texas.
□ A mouse is an animal. It's a small animal.
□ Joe is a very nice person.

a/an ... 可修饰职业等：
□ A: What's your job?
B: I'm a dentist. (而不用 I'm dentist)
□ 'What does Mark do?' 'He's an engineer.'
□ Would you like to be a teacher?
□ Beethoven was a composer.
□ Picasso was a famous painter.
□ Are you a student?

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/8f475a0b997e0f84.jpg)

party question  
bookshop foreign language  
hat bicycle 

## 名词的复数形式通常以 -s 结尾：

单数（一个） $\rightarrow$ 复数（两个或多个）

a flower → some flowers 

a train → two trains 

one week → a few weeks 

a nice place → some nice places 

this student → these students 

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/f6575c7f6fa1b745.jpg)



a flower


![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/9e3ad409b686dcbe.jpg)



some flowers


## 拼写（参见附录5）：

-s / -sh / -ch / -x → -es bus → buses dish → dishes 

church → churches 

box → boxes 

另 potato → potatoes

tomato → tomatoes 

-y → -ies baby → babies 

dictionary → dictionaries 

party → parties 

但 -ay / -ey / -oy → -ys day → days

-f / -fe → -ves 

shelf → shelves 

knife → knives 

boy → boys 

wife → wives 

## 在英语中，下列物品以复数形式出现：

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/032930c570e81ea0.jpg)



scissors


![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/e97b6019abbb3110.jpg)



glasses


![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/6e28543d843243de.jpg)


□ Do you wear glasses? 


trousers


![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/2196f5e90870c7d6.jpg)



jeans


![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/a1769597e8dc8cc2.jpg)



shorts



tights


![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/8dceeb10174618bc.jpg)



pyjamas


![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/296171298253c570.jpg)


□ Where are the scissors? I need them. 

可以说 a pair of scissors / a pair of trousers / a pair of pyjamas 等：

□ I need a new pair of jeans. 或 I need some new jeans. (而不用 a new jeans)

## 有些单词的复数形式不是以 -s 结尾：

this man → these men 

a woman → some women 

one foot → two feet 

that sheep → those sheep 

a child → many children 

a tooth → all my teeth 

a fish → a lot of fish 

a mouse → some mice 

此外还有 a person → two people / some people / a lot of people 等：

□ She's a nice person. 

但 □ They are nice people. (而不用 nice persons)

people 是复数 (= they), 因此用 people are / people have 等:

□ A lot of people speak English. (而不用 speaks)

□ I like the people here. They are very friendly. 

police 是复数：

☐ The police want to talk to anybody who saw the accident. (而不用 The police wants)

by → Units 21, 63, 109 at/on → Units 103, 106–107 介词 + -ing → Unit 112

## Unit 67

# a bottle / some water (可数名词 / 不可数名词 1)

名词分为可数名词与不可数名词。

## 可数名词

例如：(a) car (a) man (a) bottle (a) house (a) key (an) idea (an) accident 可数名词前可以用 one/two/three 等表示数量：

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/d7616143644d2d3f.jpg)


one bottle 

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/af3895ff4e4ff3b6.jpg)


two bottles 

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/ac3abfcb1882830c.jpg)



three men


![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/0d52dc1ec3ce0cb8.jpg)



four houses


可数名词有单数形式和复数形式：

单数

复数

a car the car 

my car 等

the cars 

many cars 等

□ I've got a car. 

□ New cars are very expensive. 

□ There aren't many cars in the car park. 

单数形式 (car/bottle/key 等) 不可单独使用，前面需要加上 a/an:

□ We can't get into the house without a key. (而不用 without key)

## 不可数名词

例如：water air rice salt plastic money music tennis

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/36140a8dcb7b5c87.jpg)



water


![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/8937711ae70c8d4c.jpg)



salt


![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/3ed5a139393a36c7.jpg)



money


![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/3c18a1c3f7fddfac.jpg)



music


这些单词不可用 one/two/three 等修饰：one water two musics

不可数名词只有一种形式:
money the money my money some money much money 等

□ I've got some money. 

□ There isn't much money in the box. 

□ Money isn't everything. 

不可数名词前不可用 a/an: x money x music x water

但可以说 a piece of ... / a bottle of ... 等 + 不可数名词：

a bar of chocolate 

a piece of music 

a cup of coffee 

a game of tennis

1 I haven't got watch. a watch 9 Jamaica is island. 

2 Do you like cheese? OK 10 I don't need key. 

8 Music is wonderful thing. 16 Don't go out without umbrella.

# a cake / some cake / some cakes (可数名词 / 不可数名词 2)

## a/an 与 some 比较

a/an + 可数名词单数形式 (car/apple/shoe 等):

□ I need a new car. 

□ Would you like an apple? 

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/b08f757d30b9eea7.jpg)


an apple 

some + 可数名词复数形式 (cars/apples/shoes 等):

□ I need some new shoes. 

□ Would you like some apples? 

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/a863ce84a8321d0d.jpg)


some apples 

some + 不可数名词 (water/money/music 等):

□ I need some water. 

□ Would you like some cheese?
(或 Would you like a piece of cheese?)

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/f4dfe56ada11b6d9.jpg)


some cheese 或
a piece of cheese

## 请比较 a 与 some:

□ Nicole bought a hat, some shoes and some perfume. 

☐ I read a newspaper, made some phone calls, and listened to some music. 

## 很多名词有时可数，而有时又不可数：

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/b8bbef14c87c43f8.jpg)



a cake


![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/249a645b3b10b9d7.jpg)



some cakes


![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/c21a3601a06d466c.jpg)



some cake 或 a piece of cake


![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/581099a4454087f4.jpg)



a chicken


![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/ad6f65eb6a15b0fe.jpg)



some chickens


![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/cfb25b4f5fe018e2.jpg)


some chicken 或 a piece of chicken

请比较 a paper (= a newspaper) 与 some paper:

□ I want something to read. I'm going to buy a paper. 

□ I want to make a shopping list. I need some paper / a piece of paper. (而不用 a paper)

## 应注意：

advice bread furniture hair information news weather work 

这些名词通常不可数，因此不能说 a/an ... (a-bread, an advice)，也不能用复数形式 (advice, furnitures 等)。

□ Can I talk to you? I need some advice. (而不用 an advice)

□ I'm going to buy some bread. (而不用 a bread)

□ They've got some very nice furniture in their house. (而不用 furnitures)

□ Silvia has got very long hair. (而不用 hairs)

□ I'd like some information about hotels in London. (而不用 informations)

□ Listen! I've just had some good news. (而不用 a good news)

□ It's nice weather today. (而不用 a nice weather)

□ 'Do you like your job?' 'Yes, but it's hard work.' (而不用 a hard work)

可以说 a job (但不用 a work):

□ I've got a new job. (而不用 a new work)

可数名词 / 不可数名词 1 → Unit 67 some 与 any 比较 → Unit 76

1 I bought some perfume, a hat and some shoes. 

2 I bought

1 I read a book and listened to some music. 

2 I need .... money. I want to buy .... food.

4 I'm going to open .... window to get .... fresh air. 

5 Rachel didn't eat much for lunch - only .... apple and .... bread. 

6 We live in ____ big house. There's ____ nice garden with ____ beautiful trees.

8 Listen to me carefully. I'm going to give you .... advice. 

9 I want to write a letter. I need .... paper and .... pen. 

## 68.4 从画线部分中选出正确的表达方式。

1 I'm going to buy some new shoe/shoes. (shoes is right) 

2 Martin has got brown eye/eyes. 

3 Paula has got short black hair/hairs. 

4 The tour guide gave us some information/informations about the city. 

5 We're going to buy some new chair/chairs. 

6 We're going to buy some new furniture/furnitures.

## a/an

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/6c7ef06bd3783259.jpg)


有三扇窗户，a window 可指其中任意一扇。

□ I've got a car.
(有许多车——我有一辆)

□ Can I ask a question? (有许多问题——我可以问一个吗？)

□ Is there a hotel near here? (有许多宾馆——这儿附近有吗？)

□ Paris is an interesting city. (有许多有趣的城市，巴黎就是其中之一)

□ Lisa is a student.
(有许多学生，莉萨就是其中之一)

## the

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/7150ab72ca7123b8.jpg)


只有一扇窗户，用 the window。

□ I'm going to clean the car tomorrow. (= my car) 

□ Can you repeat the question, please?
(= the question that you asked) 

□ We enjoyed our holiday. The hotel was very nice. (= our hotel) 

□ Paris is the capital of France.
(法国的首都只有一个)

□ Lisa is the youngest student in her class.
(她的班里年龄最小的学生只有一个)

## 请比较 a 与 the:

☐ I bought a jacket and a shirt. The jacket was cheap, but the shirt was expensive. (= the jacket and the shirt that I bought) 

当说话人和听话人明白谈及的人或事物的具体所指时，用 the。例如：

the door / the ceiling / the floor / the carpet / the light 等 (of a room)
the roof / the garden / the kitchen / the bathroom 等 (of a house)
the centre / the station / the airport / the town hall 等 (of a town)

□ 'Where's Tom?' 'In the kitchen.' (= the kitchen of this house or flat) 

□ Turn off the light and close the door. (= the light and the door of the room) 

☐ Do you live far from the centre?
(= the centre of your town) 

□ I'd like to speak to the manager, please. (= the manager of this shop 等)

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/d458ace06cf65a23.jpg)


## 69.1 用 a/an 或 the 填空。

1 We enjoyed our trip. The hotel was very nice. 

2 'Can I ask ....a..... question?' 'Sure. What do you want to know?' 

3 You look very tired. You need .... holiday. 

4 'Where's Tom?' 'He's in garden.' 

5 Eve is .... interesting person. You should meet her. 

6 A: Excuse me, can you tell me how to get to ____ city centre? 

B: Yes, go straight on and then take ____ next turning left. 

7 A: Shall we go out for .... meal this evening? 

B: Yes, that's ____ good idea. 

8 It's ____ nice morning. Let's go for ____ walk. 

9 Amanda is .... student. When she finishes her studies, she wants to be .... journalist. She lives with two friends in .... apartment near .... college where she is studying. .... apartment is small, but she likes it. 

10 Peter and Mary have got two children, ____ boy and ____ girl. ____ boy is seven years old, and ____ girl is three. Peter works in ____ factory. Mary hasn't got ____ job at the moment. 

## 69.2 用 a/an 或 the + 下列词语完成句子。

airport cup dictionary door floor picture

1 Don't forget to turn off light when you go out.

## Unit 70

## the

当说话人和听话人明白所谈及的人或物时，要用 the:
□ What is the name of this street? (这条街只有一个名称)
□ Who is the best player in your team? (全队只有一个最佳球员)
□ Can you tell me the time, please? (= the time now)
□ My office is on the first floor. (= the first floor of the building)

注意不能省略 the:
□ Do you live near the city centre? (而不用 near city centre)
□ Excuse me, where is the nearest bank? (而不用 where is nearest ...)

## the same

□ We live in the same street. (而不用 in same street)
□ 'Are these two books different?' 'No, they're the same.' (而不用 they're same)

## 可以说：

the sun / the moon / the world / the sky / the sea / the country
□ The sky is blue and the sun is shining.
□ Do you live in a town or in the country? 

the police / the fire brigade / the army (of a city, country 等)
□ My brother is a soldier. He's in the army.
□ What do you think of the police? Do they do a good job?

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/668621e596d4d824.jpg)


the top / the end / the middle / the left 等
□ Write your name at the top of the page.
□ My house is at the end of the street.
□ The table is in the middle of the room.
□ Do you drive on the right or on the left in your country?

the left 

( play ) the piano / the guitar / the trumpet 等 ( 演奏乐器 )
□ Paula is learning to play the piano.

the right 

the radio 

□ I listen to the radio a lot. 

the top 

the
•
middle 

the bottom 

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/e68f65ae8f30c5ff.jpg)


the Internet 

□ Do you use the Internet much? 

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/5794d51040ce80e7.jpg)


![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/7dbab685c1c8a250.jpg)


下列词语前不用 the:

television / TV 

□ I watch TV a lot. 

□ What's on television tonight? 

但 Can you turn off the television? (= the TV set)

breakfast / lunch / dinner 

□ What did you have for breakfast? (而不用 the breakfast)
□ Dinner is ready!

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/00dfa7b9addf05a4.jpg)


next / last + week/month/year/summer/Monday 等
□ I'm not working next week. (而不用 the next week)
□ Did you have a holiday last summer? (而不用 the last summer)

70.1 在下列句子中的必要处填入 the。如果句子正确，则写上 OK。

1 What is name of this street? 

2 What's on television tonight? 

the name
OK

4 Would you like to go to moon?

11 I'm going out after dinner. 

12 Internet is a good way of getting information. 

13 My sister got married last month. 

14 My dictionary is on top shelf on right. 

15 We live in country about ten miles from nearest town.

age colour problem street time

4 My shirt is dark blue and so is my jacket. My shirt and jacket are 

5 I've got no money and you've got no money. We've got

## go to work go home go to the cinema

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/770bb3dc8090be49.jpg)



She's at work.


![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/fe4e6079bdb72eef.jpg)



They're going to school.


![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/dffe34b589f5b6c2.jpg)



He's in bed.


## 通常说：

(go) to work, (be) at work, start work, finish work
□ Bye! I'm going to work now. (而不用 to the work)
□ I finish work at 5 o'clock every day.

(go) to school, (be) at school, start school, leave school 等
□ What did you learn at school today? (而不用 at the school)
□ Some children don't like school.

(go) to university/college, (be) at university/college
□ Helen wants to go to university when she leaves school.
□ What did you study at college? 

(go) to hospital, (be) in hospital
□ Jack had an accident. He had to go to hospital. 

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/bcbba9db2528718a.jpg)


(go) to prison, (be) in prison
□ Why is he in prison? What did he do? 

(go) to church, (be) in/at church
□ David usually goes to church on Sundays. 

(go) to bed, (be) in bed
□ I'm tired. I'm going to bed. (而不用 to the bed)
□ 'Where's Jane?' 'She's in bed.'

(go) home, (be) at home 等
□ I'm tired. I'm going home. (而不用 to home)
□ Are you going out tonight, or are you staying at home?

## 通常说：

(go to) the cinema / the theatre / the bank / the post office / the station / the airport / the city centre 

□ I never go to the theatre, but I go to the cinema a lot. 

□ 'Are you going to the bank?' 'No, to the post office.' 

☐ The number 5 bus goes to the airport; the number 8 goes to the city centre. 

(go to) the doctor / the dentist 

□ You're not well. Why don't you go to the doctor? 

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/898ed36ee13256c2.jpg)


□ I have to go to the dentist tomorrow.

## Unit 72

## I like music

## I hate exams

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/5a5649c501fa458e.jpg)


表示泛指时不用 the:

□ I like music, especially classical music. 

(而不用 the music ... the classical music)

□ We don't eat meat very often. (而不用 the meat)

□ Life is not possible without water.
(而不用 The life ... the water)

□ I hate exams. (而不用 the exams)

□ Do you know a shop that sells foreign newspapers? 

□ I'm not very good at writing letters. 

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/a5ddc396db992c0f.jpg)


体育活动前不用 the:

□ My favourite sports are football and skiing. (而不用 the football ... the skiing)

语言与学科名称 (history/geography/physics/biology 等) 前不用 the:

□ Do you think English is difficult? (而不用 the English)

□ Tom's brother is studying physics and chemistry. 

## 用 flowers 还是 the flowers?

## 请比较：

□ Flowers are beautiful.
(= flowers in general) 

□ I don't like cold weather. (= cold weather in general) 

□ We don't eat fish very often. (= fish in general) 

□ I love this garden.
The flowers are beautiful.
(= the flowers in this
garden) 

□ The weather isn't very good today. (= the weather today) 

□ Are you interested in history?
(= history in general) 

□ We had a great meal last night. The fish was excellent. 

(= the fish we ate last night) 

☐ Do you know much about the history of your country? 

The flowers are beautiful. 

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/09cf982410a29901.jpg)


## Exercises

## 72.1 你对下列事物是什么看法？

<table><tr><td>big cities</td><td>computer games</td><td>exams</td><td>jazz</td><td>parties</td></tr><tr><td>chocolate</td><td>dogs</td><td>housework</td><td>museums</td><td>tennis</td></tr></table>

选择其中七个，用如下句式造句：

I like ... I don't like ... I love ... I hate ... or ... is/are all right 

1 I hate exams. or I like exams. or Exams are all right. (etc.) 

## 72.2 你对下列括号内的事物感兴趣吗？用方框中的句式造句。

I'm (very) interested in ... I know a lot about ... I don't know much about ... I'm not interested in ... I know a little about ... I don't know anything about ... 

1 (history) 

2 (politics) 

3 (sport) 

4 (art) 

5 (astronomy) 

6 (economics) 

## 72.3 从画线部分中选择正确的表达方式。

1 My favourite sport is football / the football. (football is right)
2 I like this hotel. Rooms / The rooms are very nice. (The rooms is right)
3 Everybody needs friends / the friends.
4 Jane doesn't go to parties / the parties very often.
5 I went shopping this morning. Shops / The shops were very busy.
6 'Where's milk / the milk?' 'It's in the fridge.'
7 I don't like milk / the milk. I never drink it.
8 'Do you do any sports?' 'Yes, I play basketball / the basketball.'
9 'What does your brother do?' 'He sells computers / the computers.'
10 We went for a swim in the river. Water / The water was very cold.
11 I don't like swimming in cold water / the cold water.
12 Excuse me, can you pass salt / the salt, please?
13 I like this town. I like people / the people here.
14 Vegetables / The vegetables are good for you.
15 Houses / The houses in this street are all the same.
16 I can't sing this song. I don't know words / the words.
17 I enjoy taking photographs / the photographs. It's my hobby.
18 Do you want to see photographs / the photographs that I took when I was on holiday?
19 English / The English is used a lot in international business / the international business.
20 Money / The money doesn't always bring happiness / the happiness. 

## the ... (地名)

地点（大洲、国家、州、岛、城镇等）

地域名称前面一般不用 the:
□ France is a very large country. (而不用 the France)
□ Cairo is the capital of Egypt.
□ Corsica is an island in the Mediterranean.
□ Peru is in South America.

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/5959c7fbbe6a4cd7.jpg)


但 the 与带 republic / states / kingdom 等词的国名连用：
the Czech Republic
the United States of America (the USA)
the United Kingdom (the UK)

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/2e2e12e9334df7d3.jpg)


the -s (复数名词)

the 与国家、岛屿、山脉等名称的复数形式连用：
the Netherlands the Canary Islands
the Philippines the Alps

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/b67ddfa3cb40c8e8.jpg)


## 海洋、河流等

洋、海、江、河的名称前用 the:
the Atlantic (Ocean) the Mediterranean (Sea) the Amazon
the (River) Nile the Suez Canal the Black Sea

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/c50c0476257883ce.jpg)


城镇中的地点（街道、建筑等）

街道、广场等的名称前通常不用 the:
□ Kevin lives in Newton Street.
□ Where is Highfield Road, please?
□ Times Square is in New York.

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/e8d3c91bf14d5318.jpg)


机场、车站、大学、城堡等重要建筑物的名称前不用 the:
Kennedy Airport Westminster Abbey London Zoo
Victoria Station Cambridge University Edinburgh Castle

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/16f122d3c97438d1.jpg)


但通常宾馆、影院、戏院、博物馆的名称前要用 the: the Regent Hotel the National Theatre the Science Museum the Odeon (Cinema)

## the ... of ...

表示名称时可用 the ... of ... 结构:
the Museum of Modern Art the University of California
the Great Wall of China the Tower of London

也可以说 the north / the south / the east / the west (of ...): □ I've been to the north of Italy, but not to the south.

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/2eea0c1c1a68d318.jpg)

## this/that/these/those

this (单数)

Do you like this picture? 

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/117cfde32a982e90.jpg)


these (复数)

These flowers are for you. 

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/11859f0b5514c028.jpg)


that (单数)

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/59040fb0994f5456.jpg)


those (复数)

Who are those people? 

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/d705844dc3c17c30.jpg)


this
these this picture 

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/5d9ae4b021ef8b7b.jpg)


(这幅画)

these flowers 

(这些花)

that
those that picture 

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/29f2bed3f10b1eb1.jpg)


(那幅画)

(那些人)

those people 

this/that/these/those 可与名词连用 (this picture / those girls 等) 或单独使用：

□ This hotel is expensive, but it's very nice. 

□ 'Who's that girl?' 'I don't know.' 

□ Do you like these shoes? I bought them last week. 

与名词连用

□ Those apples look nice. Can I have one? 

□ This is a nice hotel, but it's very expensive. 

□ 'Excuse me, is this your bag?' 'Oh yes, thank you.' 

□ Who's that? (= Who is that person?) 

单独使用

□ Which shoes do you prefer – these or those? 

that 可指 “已发生的事”

□ 'I'm sorry I forgot to phone you.' 'That's all right.' 

☐ That was a really nice meal. Thank you very much. 

that 也可指 “某人刚说过的话”：

□ 'You're a teacher, aren't you?' 'Yes, that's right.' 

□ 'Martin has got a new job.' 'Has he? I didn't know that.' 

□ 'I'm going on holiday next week.' 'Oh, that's nice.' 

打电话时用 this is ... 与 is that ...? 结构：

□ Hi Sarah, this is David. 

(this 为说话方)

□ Is that Sarah?
(that 为听话方)

用 this is ... 结构来介绍某人：

□ A: Brian, this is Chris. 

B: Hello, Chris – nice to meet you. 

c: Hi. 

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/4b23cb1fba9f038f.jpg)


Hi Sarah,
this is David.

## 74.3 用 this is, that's 或 that 完成句子。

1 A: I'm sorry I'm late.  
B: That's all right. 

2 A: I can't come to the party tomorrow.
B: Oh, ____ a pity. Why not? 

3 on the phone
SUE: Hello, Jane. .... Sue.
JANE: Oh, hi Sue. How are you? 

4 A: You're lazy.  
B: not true! 

5 A: Beth plays the piano very well.
B: Does she? I didn't know ____ 

6 Mark meets Paul's sister, Helen.
PAUL: Mark, ____ my sister, Helen.
MARK: Hi, Helen. 

7 A: I'm sorry I was angry yesterday. B: OK. Forget it! 

8 A: You're a friend of Tim's, aren't you?
B: Yes, ____ right. 

## one/ones

## one (= a ...)

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/d15548ab0069d5ae.jpg)


Would you like one? 

= Would you like a chocolate ? 

one = a/an ... (a chocolate / an apple 等)

□ I need a pen. Have you got one? (one = a pen) 

□ A: Is there a bank near here? 

B: Yes, there's one at the end of this street. (one = a bank) 

## one 与 ones 比较

## one (单数)

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/7b119a427d1bc4f8.jpg)


Which one? = Which hat? 

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/dc6232fec6fd2940.jpg)


## one = hat/car/girl 等

## this one / that one

Which ones? = Which flowers? 

□ Which car is yours? This one or that one? (= this car 或 that car)

## the one

□ A: Which hotel did you stay at? 

B: The one opposite the station. 

□ I found this key. Is it the one you lost? 

## the ... one

□ I don't like the black coat, but I like the brown one. 

□ Don't buy that camera. Buy the other one. 

## a/an ... one

□ This cup is dirty. Can I have a clean one? 

□ That biscuit was nice. I'm going to have another one. 

## ones = flowers/cars/girls 等

these/those 或 these ones / those ones

□ Which flowers do you want?
These or those? 或
These ones or those ones?

## the ones ...

□ A: Which books are yours?
B: The ones on the table. 

□ I found these keys. Are they the ones you lost? 

## the ... ones

□ I don't like the red shoes, but I like the green ones. 

□ Don't buy those apples. Buy the other ones. 

## some ... ones

☐ These cups are dirty. Can we have some clean ones? 

□ My shoes are very old. I'm going to buy some new ones.

## better big clean different new old
